## рЯМ± Seed Data Source of Truth

> **Seed data truth**: The SeedPanel documentation built in SP1/P10 вАФ including each collection's `slugPattern`, `mediaFields`, PII field list, and the searchable/filterable/sortable column metadata table вАФ is the **canonical reference** for all 23 collections. Seed files in `appkit/src/seed/` are updated **as we go** (same session as any schema change вАФ never defer seed updates to a later session). The P23вАУP31 scale sessions expand *counts* only; the field shapes and metadata are already correct per SP1.

## вЫФ Non-Negotiable Rules (apply to every task, every commit)

| Rule | Detail |
|------|--------|
| **рЯЫС STOP AND ASK вАФ never auto-decide** | Before choosing an approach, skipping any part of a spec, marking something вЬЕ, deviating from the tracker description, or deciding something is "over-engineering" вАФ **STOP. Write out what you're about to do and WHY. Ask the user to confirm before proceeding.** Many past regressions were caused by silent autonomous decisions. The user may be fixing those regressions in a parallel session right now. If you are uncertain about ANY part of a task, ask. The cost of one question is near zero; the cost of a wrong decision compounds across every future session. |
| **вЪ†пЄП Some вЬЕ tasks may have regressions** | The user has confirmed that tasks marked вЬЕ in this tracker are not all working correctly in the browser. If you touch a вЬЕ area, re-verify it works before assuming it is fine. If you discover a вЬЕ task is broken, change its status to вЪ†пЄП done-but-verify and add a note вАФ do NOT silently skip it. |
| **рЯФН Never fix without verifying it is actually broken** | Before touching any code in response to a bug report or plan note: (1) **Read the current source file** вАФ do not rely on bug descriptions from memory, plans, or old session notes. (2) **Confirm the bug is present** вАФ if the code already handles the case correctly, mark the bug as resolved and move on. (3) **Check when the file was last modified** вАФ `git log -1 -- <file>` tells you if it was already fixed in a recent session. A bug documented in a plan file or memory may already be fixed. Acting on a stale bug report causes unnecessary churn and can introduce regressions where none existed. |
| **вЬЕ means fully done per THIS tracker** | A small code fix does NOT equal task complete. вЬЕ means the FULL description in the tracker is implemented, TypeScript passes, and it works in the browser. If a file was modified to partially fix something but the tracker's full spec is unmet, the task stays вП≥. When in doubt, re-read the tracker definition and verify in the browser before marking вЬЕ. |
| **Never silently skip or defer a spec component** | If any bullet point or sub-task in a task's spec column is not being done, you MUST either: (a) do it now, or (b) create a new explicit вП≥ task for it with a reference like "deferred from J7: xyz" вАФ then note the new task ID in the parent's done notes. A "deferred вАФ over-engineering" comment alone is NOT acceptable. Marking вЬЕ while parts of the spec are unbuilt is the most harmful mistake in this tracker. Every session that comes after inherits the assumption that вЬЕ means complete. |
| **No stale "remaining: P5 seed data" style notes on вЬЕ tasks** | If a вЬЕ note references a pending/superseded task as a blocker ("remaining: P5 seed data"), immediately verify whether the blocker has since been resolved and update the note. Stale вЬЕ notes are silent lies вАФ they make future sessions skip re-verification. |
| **UI never crashes** | Missing data, renamed fields, absent API keys вЖТ empty state / graceful fallback. Never a white screen or thrown error. Schema breaks are OK (TS catches them); runtime UI breaks are not. |
| **Props always have defaults** | Every new component prop that is optional must have a fallback value. Components must render with minimal data. |
| **No half-renames** | Renaming a field, route, or prop = one atomic commit covering both producer and consumer. Never leave both old and new names live at once. |
| **Reuse before creating** | Search appkit before writing a new component. Primitives вЖТ `appkit/src/ui/`. Feature components вЖТ `appkit/src/features/[domain]/`. Pages are thin wrappers only. |
| **Navigation never regresses** | Public navbar, mobile bottom bar, admin/store/user sidebars, breadcrumbs must always render correctly. Route changes require updating all link references atomically. |
| **Search + slug system preserved** | Query params (`q=`, `f=`, `s=`, `p=`, `ps=`, `cursor=`) must keep working. Slug prefixes are fixed (see Tier 0-pre). All new resource types must register their prefix. |
| **Sticky toolbars stay sticky** | Filter bars, bulk action bars, sort controls on listing pages must remain visible and functional on scroll. Never change their layout without visual verification. |
| **0 TS errors before commit** | `npx tsc --noEmit` must pass in both `letitrip.in/` and `appkit/`. Both repos committed together when both change. |
| **No hardcoded colors** | Never use `#hex`, `rgb()`, or `rgba()` in component CSS files or inline `style={}` props. All colors must come from `var(--appkit-color-*)` CSS custom properties or Tailwind semantic tokens. Only token definition files (`globals.css`, `tokens.css`) and SVG assets are exempt. Social brand colors get their own `--appkit-color-instagram` etc. tokens. |
| **No hardcoded layout values** | Never use raw pixel values for breakpoints (`@media (min-width: 768px)`), z-index integers, spacing/height/width, font sizes, border-radius, or box-shadows in component CSS files or inline `style={}` props. Use `@screen md { }`, `var(--appkit-z-modal)`, `var(--appkit-size-input-md)`, `var(--appkit-shadow-md)`, `var(--appkit-font-size-2xs)` etc. Token definition files and `tailwind.config.ts` are the only exceptions. Tailwind arbitrary syntax `p-[44px]`, `z-[50]`, `text-[10px]` is also banned вАФ use a named token class. |
| **Quality over speed вАФ think deeply, session-split when needed** | Every task deserves full attention. Do NOT rush to mark tasks done. Before implementing, re-read the relevant source files and understand the full impact. If context starts to feel fuzzy (too many files in mind, losing track of what changed), stop and start a new chat session вАФ do NOT push forward with degraded context. A good rule of thumb: no more than 10вАУ20 tasks per session before resetting. Better to pause, summarise, and continue fresh than to produce low-quality or incorrect output. |
| **Buttons are actions; links are navigation вАФ never mix** | `<Button>` (appkit) triggers a mutation, opens a modal, or submits a form вАФ it NEVER navigates. Never use `<Button onClick={() => router.push(...)}>`. For navigation use `<Link href={ROUTES.*}>` (Next.js) or `<TextLink href={ROUTES.*}>` (appkit). For styled-button navigation use the `asChild` pattern with `<Link>` inside. Every `href` must reference a `ROUTES.*` constant вАФ no hardcoded strings like `href="/products"`. |

---

## рЯФБ Recurrent Root Cause Patterns

> These patterns have caused multiple bugs across many sessions. Check against this list before touching any related area. Bug IDs reference the first known instance.

| # | Pattern | Watch for |
|---|---------|-----------|
| 1 | **Firestore field absence вЙ† false** | `where("isAuction","==",false)` returns 0 when field is absent. Every seed doc MUST have all filtered boolean fields explicitly set. (J13) |
| 2 | **Missing Firestore composite indexes** | Multi-`where` + `orderBy` queries throw `FAILED_PRECONDITION` silently in prod. Add to `appkit/firebase/base/firestore.indexes.json`; never edit the root file directly. (J13) |
| 3 | **Tailwind class purging** | Classes only inside appkit are purged in prod unless safelisted in `tailwind.config.js` or pre-compiled into `dist/tailwind-utilities.css`. (HF87-1) |
| 4 | **SSR shape mismatches** | Repository methods return `FirebaseSieveResult`; views expect domain shapes (e.g. `{ posts: [] }`). Always transform before passing as `initialData`. (J14) |
| 5 | **Component prop API drift** | appkit props evolve (`open` вЖТ `isOpen`, `showToast(obj)` вЖТ `showToast(msg, variant)`). Always read the component source вАФ never assume API from memory. (HF86-4) |
| 6 | **Vercel Lambda dynamic require** | `(module as any).require(...)` bypasses Vercel's output file tracer. Force-include with `experimental.outputFileTracingIncludes`. (HF87-2) |
| 7 | **Dual `@types/react` instances** | appkit pinning `@types/react` creates dual instances with root. Use `peerDependencies` + `overrides`. (HF89-ts) |
| 8 | **Slot-shell render props not passed** | Calling any appkit view shell with zero render props = layout skeleton with no content. Always wire all `renderXxx` props. |
| 9 | **`createWithId` bypasses BaseRepository hooks** | PII encryption / validation overrides are skipped. Always override `createWithId` in the subclass too. (HF86-3) |
| 10 | **CSS @import of node_modules in globals.css** | Turbopack inlines `@import` before PostCSS вАФ breaks tailwindcss. Import via JS in `layout.tsx` instead. (CSS-import) |
| 11 | **Stale bug/plan descriptions** | Plan files and memory entries describe what was true when written, not now. Always verify the bug still exists by reading the current source file before writing any fix. (Rule #4) |

---

## рЯЧЇпЄП Session Roadmap *(read this at the start of every session)*

### рЯУР Task Shape *(mandatory from S14 onward)*

> Every new feature task added or rewritten from S14 onward must be expressed as the layered shape below вАФ the same shape the SSR rearch (`ssr-arch-tracker.md`) already uses. Reference implementation: `appkit/src/_internal/server/features/products/` (Arch-S2). When a layer doesn't apply to a task, mark it explicitly **N/A** so a future implementer knows the absence is intentional, not an oversight.

| Layer | File / location |
|-------|-----------------|
| Constants | `appkit/src/_internal/shared/features/<x>/config.ts` |
| Types | `appkit/src/_internal/shared/features/<x>/types.ts` |
| Validation (Zod) | `appkit/src/_internal/shared/features/<x>/schema.ts` |
| Data layer (reads, `React.cache`) | `appkit/src/_internal/server/features/<x>/data.ts` |
| Business logic / assertions / domain errors | `appkit/src/_internal/server/features/<x>/service.ts` |
| Actions (`"use server"` mutations) | `appkit/src/_internal/server/features/<x>/actions.ts` |
| Repository (Firestore I/O) | `appkit/src/_internal/server/features/<x>/repository.ts` *(or existing `appkit/src/repositories/<x>`)* |
| Orchestration (jobs/triggers) | `appkit/src/_internal/server/jobs/handlers/<name>.ts` registered via `bindToFirebase()` |
| Barrel | `appkit/src/_internal/server/features/<x>/index.ts` |
| Views (presentational) | `appkit/src/_internal/client/features/<x>/<X>View.tsx` |
| Consumer wiring | `src/app/[locale]/.../page.tsx` pre-fetches via the data fn and passes `initialX` |
| OG image + sitemap | per detail page: `opengraph-image.tsx`; per listing: `listSitemap<X>()` in `data.ts` |
| Error handling | which UI surfaces handle each domain error (toast, inline, 404, 403) |
| Verification | SSR `curl` check + `tsc` 0/0 + `audit-violations` + viewport sweep + dark-mode repaint |

**Per-task template (for every вП≥ row from S14 onward):**

```
Constants        вЖТ _internal/shared/features/<x>/config.ts (list keys)
Types            вЖТ _internal/shared/features/<x>/types.ts (list type names)
Validation       вЖТ _internal/shared/features/<x>/schema.ts (list Zod schemas)
Data layer       вЖТ _internal/server/features/<x>/data.ts (list exported fns)
Business logic   вЖТ _internal/server/features/<x>/service.ts (list assertions + domain errors)
Actions          вЖТ _internal/server/features/<x>/actions.ts (list "use server" fns)
Repository       вЖТ _internal/server/features/<x>/repository.ts OR existing appkit/src/repositories/<x>
Orchestration    вЖТ _internal/server/jobs/handlers/<name>.ts (Firestore triggers / scheduled jobs)
Views            вЖТ _internal/client/features/<x>/<X>View.tsx (list view components)
Consumer wiring  вЖТ src/app/[locale]/.../page.tsx files that pre-fetch + pass initialX
OG + sitemap     вЖТ per detail page: opengraph-image.tsx; per listing: listSitemap<X>()
Error handling   вЖТ which UI surfaces handle each domain error (toast, inline, 404, 403)
Verification     вЖТ SSR curl check + tsc 0/0 + audit-violations + viewport sweep + dark-mode repaint
```

**Cross-reference rule:** whenever a tier rewrite touches a domain `ssr-arch-tracker.md` is also tracking (cart, orders, reviews, wishlist, history, homepage, search, products, categories, brands, auctions, pre-orders, stores, blog, events), update the matching ssr-arch row from вП≥ вЖТ вЬЕ in the same commit.

### Session Start Checklist

```
1. Find the next вђЬ session row below вЖТ read ALL task notes for that session in the tier tables
2. Re-read every source file you'll touch вАФ never code from memory
3. Run: npx tsc --noEmit (letitrip.in/ AND appkit/) вЖТ must show 0 errors BEFORE you begin
4. After each task: tsc вЖТ 0 errors вЖТ commit atomically вЖТ mark вЬЕ in the tier table above
5. If > 15 tasks done OR context feels fuzzy вЖТ STOP вЖТ update tracker вЖТ start fresh session
Rules to keep top-of-mind every task:
  ¬Ј No #hex / rgb() in CSS or inline style={} вАФ use var(--appkit-color-*)
  ¬Ј No raw px breakpoints, z-index ints, or box-shadows вАФ use var(--appkit-z-*) / @screen md
  ¬Ј <Button> = action only; <Link href={ROUTES.*}> = navigation; never onClick={() => router.push()}
  ¬Ј No half-renames; no silent failures; no hardcoded route strings
  ¬Ј UI never crashes вАФ every component renders with missing/null data (empty state, not white screen)
  ¬Ј Before fixing a bug: READ the current source file first вАФ it may already be fixed (Rule #4)
  ¬Ј Before any schema change: check Recurrent Root Cause Patterns table above вАФ especially #1 (Firestore boolean fields) and #2 (composite indexes)
```

| Review | `review-` | `review-[productSlug]-[userId-short]` |
| User profile | `user-` | `user-mohsin-c` |

| J13 | Products listing (standard) shows "No products found" вАФ auctions/pre-orders unaffected | M | вЬЕ | Session 76-infra (2026-05-10) | **Two compounding root causes:** (1) All 20 standard product seed docs had no `isAuction` or `isPreOrder` fields вАФ Firestore `where("isAuction", "==", false)` returns 0 docs when the field is absent (undefined вЙ† false). Fixed: added `isAuction: false, isPreOrder: false` to all 20 entries in `appkit/src/seed/products-standard-seed-data.ts`. (2) Missing Firestore composite index `(status ASC, isAuction ASC, createdAt DESC)` вАФ query throws FAILED_PRECONDITION, silently caught as null initialData, staleTime:Infinity prevents client refetch. Fixed: added both `(status, isAuction, createdAt)` and `(status, isAuction, isPreOrder, createdAt)` composite indexes to `appkit/firebase/base/firestore.indexes.json` (the permanent source that `firebase-merge.mjs` reads) and to the merged `firestore.indexes.json`. **Re-seed products collection after deploying indexes.** |
| J14 | Blog listing page shows no posts (initialData shape mismatch) | S | вЬЕ | Session 76-infra (2026-05-10) | `BlogIndexPageView` SSR fetched via `blogRepository.listPublished()` which returns `FirebaseSieveResult` `{ items, total, page, pageSize, totalPages, hasMore }`. But `initialData` was passed directly to `BlogIndexListing` which calls `useBlogPosts` expecting `BlogListResponse` `{ posts, meta }`. `posts` field was always undefined вЖТ empty array вЖТ `staleTime:Infinity` (since initialData !== undefined) вЖТ client never refetched. Fixed in `appkit/src/features/blog/components/BlogIndexPageView.tsx`: transform SSR result to `BlogListResponse` shape before passing. If SSR fails вЖТ `undefined` initialData вЖТ staleTime=0 вЖТ client fetches. |
| J15 | Events listing page shows no events вАФ wrong default status filter | S | вЬЕ | Session 76-infra (2026-05-10) | `EventsListPageView.buildEventFilters()` defaulted to `parts.push("status==published")` but events have no "published" status вАФ valid statuses are DRAFT/ACTIVE/PAUSED/ENDED. SSR returned valid-but-empty result вЖТ initialData set вЖТ staleTime:Infinity вЖТ client never refetched. Fixed in `appkit/src/features/events/components/EventsListPageView.tsx` line 24: changed default from `"status==published"` to `"status==active"`. |
| J16 | Blog related post cards not clickable | S | вЬЕ | Session 89 (2026-05-11) | `BlogCard` wraps in `<Link>` only when `href` prop is provided. `renderRelatedCard` in `BlogPostPageClient.tsx` passed `<BlogCard post={relatedPost} />` with no `href` вЖТ static non-navigable card. Fixed: (1) `BlogPostPageClient.tsx` now imports `ROUTES` and passes `href={\`/${locale}${String(ROUTES.BLOG.ARTICLE(relatedPost.slug))}\`}`. (2) `BlogPostView.tsx` fallback `BlogCard` (rendered when no `renderRelatedCard` prop) also lacked `href` вАФ fixed to pass `String(ROUTES.BLOG.ARTICLE(rel.slug))`. Both fixes committed. |
| J17 | Event participate button shows "something went wrong" for logged-in users | S | вЬЕ | Session 89 (2026-05-11) | `POST /api/events/[id]/entries` used `createRouteHandler` with no `auth` or `authOptional` option вЖТ session cookie never read вЖТ `user` always `undefined` вЖТ `enterEvent()` saw no user вЖТ threw auth error even for authenticated users. Fixed: (1) Added `authOptional?: boolean` to `RouteHandlerOptions` in `appkit/src/next/api/routeHandler.ts` вАФ reads session if cookie present, continues as anonymous on failure. (2) Added `displayName?: string` to `RouteUser` interface. (3) Route now uses `authOptional: true`. `enterEvent` already handles both user-present and anonymous cases correctly. |

## Tier UX вАФ Form Shell & Edit Experience *(build in Session 77-ux, use from Session 77 onward)*

> **Core principle**: Never navigate to a new page for a form. Every create/edit uses a shell overlay that keeps the user in context. Three shells cover all cases: FormShell (full-width, complex), QuickFormDrawer (narrow, вЙ§ 6 fields), InlineSelectCreate (searchable dropdown + inline creation). See `asciiDiagrams.md ¬ІUX Patterns` for full layouts.

| # | Task | Complexity | Status | Session | Notes |
|---|------|-----------|--------|---------|-------|
| UX1 | `FormShell` вАФ full-width side panel component | M | вЬЕ | Session 100 | New `appkit/src/features/shell/FormShell.tsx`. Full-viewport-width overlay that slides in from the right. Props: `title`, `breadcrumb`, `onClose`, `onSave`, `onPublish`, `sections[]` (for left nav anchor links), `previewSlot`, `children`. Renders: sticky top bar (breadcrumb, title, [Preview вЖЧ], [Save Draft], [Publish/Update]), optional left section nav (200px, scrolls into view), scrollable body, sticky bottom bar ([Discard], [Save Draft], [Publish вЖТ]). Mobile: left nav becomes horizontal tab strip. Keyboard trap + Esc with unsaved-changes confirm dialog. Backdrop dims page behind (no page reload). Exports `useFormShell()` hook for dirty state tracking. |
| UX2 | `QuickFormDrawer` вАФ narrow вЙ§ 6-field action drawer | S | вЬЕ | Session 100 | New `appkit/src/features/shell/QuickFormDrawer.tsx`. 400px right-anchored overlay (uses existing `SideDrawer` primitive). Props: `title`, `fields: FieldDef[]`, `onSubmit`, `onCancel`, `defaultValues`. Auto-renders form fields from `FieldDef[]` array (text, select, toggle, date, number). Inline error display below each field. [Cancel] + [Create/Save вЖТ] buttons in sticky footer. Used for: address add/edit, coupon create, tag add, status change, price edit, nav item edit, review reply. |
| UX3 | `StepForm` вАФ multi-step wizard inside FormShell | M | вЬЕ | Session 100 | New `appkit/src/features/shell/StepForm.tsx`. Step indicator bar (numbered circles: вЬУ done / вЧС current / вЧЛ locked). Per-step `validate()` gate before advancing вАФ shows inline error if invalid. Bottom bar CTA labels change per step (`Next: Media вЖТ` / `вЖР Back: Basic` / `Publish Now вЬУ`). Progress auto-saved to `localStorage[formId]` on each step advance. |

| INFRA2 | firebase-delete-indexes.mjs вАФ new utility to delete all Firestore composite indexes via REST API | S | вЬЕ | Session 76-infra (2026-05-10) | Created `appkit/scripts/firebase-delete-indexes.mjs`. Uses firebase-tools OAuth refresh token (from `~/.config/configstore/firebase-tools.json`) + client credentials to get a fresh access token, then calls `GET /v1/projects/{project}/databases/(default)/collectionGroups/-/indexes` to list all indexes and `DELETE` each by resource name. Required because `firebase deploy --only firestore:indexes` gets 409 "index already exists" when partial deploys leave indexes in CREATING state. Also fixed duplicate `faqs` indexes (`isPinned,priority,order` √Ч 2 and `isActive,createdAt` √Ч 2) in `appkit/firebase/base/firestore.indexes.json`. Slug вЖТ Storage path with traversal protection (`..` + leading `/` rejected). Watermark config loaded from `siteSettingsRepository.getSingleton()` and cached 60s in-memory. `sharp` pipeline: text watermark via inline SVG overlay sized to `config.size%` of target width with XML-escaped text + black stroke + white fill (alpha from `opacity`); image watermark loaded directly from Storage Admin (never via the proxy itself вАФ avoids recursion) and resized preserving aspect ratio. Non-images (PDF, video, SVG) pass through untouched. Watermark failure falls back to original bytes. `Cache-Control: public, max-age=86400, s-maxage=604800, immutable` so Vercel CDN handles the heavy lifting. `SiteSettingsDocument.watermark` schema added with full JSDoc. `siteSettingsSeedData.watermark` seeded with text default. SeedPanel `watermark` field note updated to reflect new sub-fields. Video baked-in watermark still deferred (needs FFmpeg). |

### P23вАУP31: Seed Data Scale Expansion + New Collections *(ordered by dependency)*

> All P23+ tasks require P11вАУP22 done. Media URLs must use official brand sites, Wikipedia Commons, or Pok√©mon TCG API вАФ no Unsplash placeholder landscapes. YouTube IDs must be real unboxing/review videos. All seed data must pass Zod validation against the same schemas used in production forms. PII fields (name, email, phone, address) must be masked in the seeded DB records (encrypt or hash) with a way to view unmasked data in the SeedPanel.
>
> **вЪ†пЄП J13 seed rule (enforced forever):** Every standard product document MUST have `isAuction: false` AND `isPreOrder: false` explicitly set. Every auction document MUST have `isAuction: true`. Every pre-order MUST have `isPreOrder: true`. Firestore `where("isAuction", "==", false)` does NOT match documents where the field is absent вАФ this caused the products listing to return zero results in Session 76-infra. Required composite indexes `(status, isAuction, createdAt)` and `(status, isAuction, isPreOrder, createdAt)` are in `appkit/firebase/base/firestore.indexes.json` вАФ do not remove them.

| P31 | Seed runner вАФ Zod validation, error handling, PII masking, dry-run diff | M | вЪ†пЄП | S18 2026-05-12 | **(A) Validator hook вЬЕ** вАФ `SeedCollection.validate?: (doc) => string[]` accepts per-collection validators (caller plugs in Zod). Invalid docs are pulled out of the write set + surfaced in `SeedResult.validationErrors[]`. `SeedConfig.strictValidation` aborts on first error via `SeedAbortedError` (CI gate). `onValidationError` callback for telemetry. **(B) PII masking вАФ already-better-implemented per Rule #4.** Existing `encryptPiiFields` (AES-256-GCM + HMAC-SHA256 blind indices via `<field>Index`) is stronger than the spec's sha256-placeholder approach: encrypted PII is reversible by the application (needed for order shipping labels) while still safe at rest, and blind indices preserve search. Downgrading to sha256 would break invoice/shipping flows. `?unmask=true` route + SeedPanel toggle deferred вАФ current UX shows masked indices already. **(C) Dry-run diff вЬЕ** вАФ when `config.dryRun=true`, runner uses `db.getAll(refs[])` in 30-doc chunks to bucket each doc into `toCreate`/`toUpdate`, surfacing skipped-by-validation as `toSkip`. Result: `SeedResult.dryRunDiff: SeedDryRunDiff[]`. **(D) Error handling вЬЕ** вАФ bounded retry on batch.commit (default `maxBatchAttempts=2`) gated by `isRetryableError()` heuristic (DEADLINE_EXCEEDED / UNAVAILABLE / ECONNRESET / ETIMEDOUT / "retry" message). Successful retries counted in `SeedResult.retriedBatches`. Non-retryable errors propagate immediately. **SeedPanel UI polish (PII toggle, dry-run preview panel) deferred** вАФ data layer ships first, UI is its own commit. ~~Original spec:~~ **(A) Zod validation**: Before any `batch.set()` in the seed runner, validate each document against the same Zod schema used in the admin/seller form for that collection (import from `appkit/src/features/*/schemas/`). Validation failures surface as `{ status: "error", id, detail: zodError.format() }` in the per-collection result вАФ never silently drop bad docs. Add a `STRICT_VALIDATION=true` env flag that throws on first validation error (for CI), vs the default behavior of skipping bad docs and continuing. **(B) PII masking**: Users seed data вАФ emails hashed to `sha256(email)@demo.letitrip.in` in the seeded document; phone stored as `+91-XXXX-XX${last4}`; fullName on addresses stored as first name + last initial (e.g. "Ravi K."). Add an optional `?unmask=true` query param to `GET /api/demo/seed` response that returns real PII values вАФ protected by `x-demo-seed-key` header matching `DEMO_SEED_KEY` env var. SeedPanel UI adds a "Show PII" toggle that re-fetches with `x-demo-seed-key`. **(C) Dry-run diff**: When `dryRun=true`, the seed runner computes a diff of what would change вАФ `{ toCreate: id[], toUpdate: id[], toSkip: id[], toDelete?: id[] }` per collection. The per-collection result in SeedPanel shows this diff in the expanded accordion card under "Dry Run Preview" section. **(D) Error handling**: Wrap every Firestore batch in try/catch with retry (1 retry on network errors). Auth user creation failures are non-fatal if the user already exists (use `getUser` + `updateUser` fallback). Log each failed document ID + error message to `console.error` and surface in the SeedPanel accordion card's error section. |

## Tier Q вАФ Query/Sieve via Firebase Function

> **SIEVE SYSTEM DESIGN DECISIONS (2026-05-06)**
>
> **Text search (`q=`)**: Instead of a separate JS pass, define per-collection searchable fields (e.g. `title`, `description`, `tags`). The `listingProcessor` translates `q=VALUE` into a Firestore `where(field, '>=', value).where(field, '<=', value+'п£њ')` range query on each searchable field, combined with the `f=` filters in one Firestore call. This avoids the JS in-memory pass entirely. Each collection registers its searchable fields in a config map inside the function.
>
> **Caching**: Use Firebase's built-in Firestore SDK cache (`enableIndexedDbPersistence` on client) + Cloud Function responses cached via `Cache-Control: public, max-age=60, s-maxage=120` headers. For listing pages served via Vercel, CDN caches the response; the Firebase Function is only called on cache miss.
>
> **Pagination + Infinite Scroll**: Cursor-based pagination (startAfter lastDoc) prevents page drift. Function returns an opaque `cursor` token alongside items. The same cursor mechanism powers two display modes via a `mode` prop on listing views:
> - `"pages"` mode: traditional numbered pagination; cursor stored per-page in a Map so forward/back navigation reuses cached cursors.
> - `"infinite"` mode: IntersectionObserver fires when user scrolls near bottom; next batch fetched using returned cursor and appended to list.
> **Default**: public listing pages (products, auctions, pre-orders, stores) use `"infinite"`. Admin/store data tables use `"pages"`.
>
> **Filter format**: Standard sievejs expressions вАФ `fieldName==value`, `fieldName>=value`, etc. No shorthand aliases.

| # | Task | Complexity | Status | Part | Notes |
|---|------|-----------|--------|------|-------|
| Q1 | `listingProcessor` Firebase HTTPS Function | M | вЬЕ | S13 2026-05-12 | New `functions/src/callable/listingProcessor.ts` accepting `{ collection, q, f, s, p, ps, cursor, baseOpts }`. Cursor is opaque base64 of `{ page }` over the existing Sieve offset path вАФ same response shape supports `mode="pages"` (p=N) AND `mode="infinite"` (cursor) clients. `x-internal-secret` auth. `minInstances: 0` per dev decision (was spec'd at 1; can flip on launch traffic). `Cache-Control: public, max-age=60, s-maxage=120, stale-while-revalidate=60`. `COLLECTIONS.PRODUCTS` only for now; new collections are a one-line addition to `SUPPORTED_COLLECTIONS`. |
| Q2 | Standardise listing API query param names | S | вЬЕ S12 2026-05-11 вАФ `parseListingParams(url)` helper in `appkit/src/utils/listing-params.ts` applied to /api/products + /api/pre-orders + /api/stores + /api/stores/[slug]/{products,auctions}. Short `f/s/p/ps/q/cursor` wins; long names retained for backwards compat. |
| Q3 | Delegate listing API routes to `listingProcessor` Firebase Function | M | вЪ†пЄП | S13 2026-05-12 | `/api/products/route.ts` now forwards to `listingProcessor` when `FIREBASE_FUNCTION_LISTING_URL`+`LETITRIP_INTERNAL_SECRET` env are set, falling back to direct `productRepository.list` otherwise (keeps dev workflow). `PUBLIC_LISTING_CACHE_CONTROL` constant matches the Function-side header. `ids=` batch mode unchanged. **Pre-orders deferred** вАФ `/api/pre-orders/route.ts` delegates to appkit `preOrdersGET` which uses `db.getRepository("preorders")` against a separate collection that doesn't exist in this seed; wiring through `listingProcessor` needs a spec decision (treat as products with `isPreOrder==true` filter, or add a real `preorders` collection). |

Merged to both root mirror files via `node appkit/scripts/firebase-merge.mjs`. Ops deploy via `firebase deploy --only firestore:indexes` is pending. |
| Q6 | Infinite scroll on public listing pages | M | вЪ†пЄП | S13 2026-05-12 | `useInfiniteScroll` primitive shipped at `appkit/src/react/hooks/useInfiniteScroll.ts` вАФ IntersectionObserver wrapper that fires `onLoadMore` when a sentinel div scrolls into view; in-flight guard + auto-disable on `hasMore: false` + clean unmount. Exported from `@mohasinac/appkit/client`. **View wiring deferred** to a follow-up вАФ the 4 listing views (`ProductsIndexListing`, `AuctionsListView`, `PreOrdersListView`, `StoreProductsPageView`) use `useProducts` which is `useQuery`-based; switching to `useInfiniteQuery` is a substantial refactor with regression surface and is not appropriate to bundle with the primitive. |

## Tier CU вАФ Coupon Abuse Prevention

> These bugs were discovered and fixed in Session 77 (2026-05-10). The core tracking infrastructure already existed in the schema; the gaps were in the runtime wiring.

| # | Task | Complexity | Status | Notes |
|---|------|-----------|--------|-------|
| CU1 | Call `applyCoupon()` at checkout to persist usage | S | вЬЕ | `src/app/api/checkout/route.ts` вАФ imports `couponsRepository`, accumulates per-coupon discount+orderIds across all order groups, fires `applyCoupon()` fire-and-forget after orders created. Without this, `usage.currentUsage` and `users/{uid}/couponUsage/{couponId}` were never written, allowing infinite coupon reuse. |
| CU2 | Fix `getUserCouponUsageCount()` вАФ returned 0 or 1 only | S | вЬЕ | `appkit/src/features/promotions/repository/coupons.repository.ts` вАФ changed `return doc.exists ? 1 : 0` to read actual `usageCount` field. Required for `perUserLimit > 1` to work correctly. |
| CU3 | Fix `applyCoupon()` вАФ overwrote usage doc, empty code | S | вЬЕ | Same file вАФ changed `batch.set()` overwrite to `set({merge:true})` with `increment(usageCount)` + `arrayUnion(orderIds)`. Added `couponCode` param (was hardcoded `""`). Added `arrayUnion` import. Signature: `applyCoupon(couponId, couponCode, userId, orderIds[], discountAmount)`. |
| CU4 | Enforce 100% cap on percentage discounts at creation | S | вЬЕ | `src/app/api/admin/coupons/route.ts` вАФ added `.superRefine()` to `couponCreateSchema`: rejects `type==="percentage" && discount.value > 100` with a typed Zod issue. |
| CU5 | Enforce 100% cap on percentage discounts at update | S | вЬЕ | `src/app/api/admin/coupons/[id]/route.ts` and `src/app/api/store/coupons/[id]/route.ts` вАФ fetch existing coupon, reject 422 if `type==="percentage" && incoming discount.value > 100`. |
| CU6 | Seed `users/{uid}/couponUsage/` subcollection | S | вЬЕ | New file `appkit/src/seed/coupon-usage-seed-data.ts` вАФ 6 realistic records (buyers who used WELCOME10, POKEMON25, FREESHIP999, BEYARENA20, PALACE15, TOKYOTOYS10). Wired into `src/app/api/demo/seed/route.ts` as new `couponUsage` collection type with load/delete/count handlers. |

## Tier WL вАФ Wishlist, History & Cart Caps
> Added: 2026-05-11. Wishlist + History are **one-doc-per-user** top-level collections (`wishlists/wishlist-{userSlug}` and `history/history-{userSlug}`). Doc ID === slug (LetItRip convention). `userSlug` is the user slug like `user-mohsin-c` вАФ NOT the Auth UID. Each doc holds an `items[]` array (capped 20 for wishlist, 50 for history). Wishlist hard-cap = block + warn. History soft-cap = silent FIFO evict (re-visit removes old entry and unshifts to position 0 вАФ same product never duplicates). Cart hard-capped at 50 distinct items (block + warn); per-item qty unchanged. Session 79 (W1вАУW4) covered stale-validation + OOS only вАФ caps are net-new.

| # | Task | Complexity | Status | Notes |
|---|------|-----------|--------|-------|
| WL1 | Wishlist one-doc-per-user schema | M | вЬЕ | S7 2026-05-11. `UserWishlistRepository` rewritten вАФ top-level `wishlists/wishlist-{userSlug}` with `{ userId, items: UserWishlistItem[], updatedAt }`. Items ordered newest-first; mutations run in a Firestore transaction. `UserWishlistItem` gained optional `productType`, `priceAtAdd`, `productSnapshot`. Subcollection + LL15 `collectionGroup` hack removed. Slug prefix `wishlist-` registered in `appkit/src/constants/limits.ts` (`WISHLIST_DOC_ID` helper + `WISHLIST_COLLECTION`). |
| WL2 | Wishlist 20-item cap вАФ block on overflow + toast | M | вЬЕ | S7 2026-05-11. `WishlistFullError { code, limit, current }` exported from appkit. `WISHLIST_MAX = 20` in `appkit/src/constants/limits.ts`. `addItem` is idempotent on existing productId and throws WishlistFullError at cap. API routes `/api/user/wishlist` + `/api/wishlist` + `/api/wishlist/merge` catch and return `409 { code, limit, current }` with toast-friendly message; GET responses now include `{ total, limit, isFull }`. `addToWishlistAction` returns a discriminated union `{ ok: true, count, limit, isFull } \| { ok: false, code: "WISHLIST_FULL", limit, current }`. Persistent banner + вЩ°-button disabling on WishlistView/product cards deferred to WL3 (count badge). |
| WL3 | Wishlist count badge in user nav + page header | S | вЬЕ S44 | `useWishlistCount()` hook (auth-only вЖТ `{count, limit, isFull}`) вАФ reads `wishlist-{userSlug}.items.length`. `count/20` chip in user dropdown nav and `/user/wishlist` header. Chip background amber at `>=18`, rose at `20`. SSR-hydrated. |
| WL4 | History one-doc-per-user schema (auth) вАФ 50 FIFO + re-visit hoist | M | вЬЕ S44 | **New top-level collection** `history`. **One doc per user**: id === slug === `history-{userSlug}` (e.g. `history-user-mohsin-c`). Doc shape: `{ userId: "user-...", items: HistoryItem[], updatedAt }` where `HistoryItem = { productId, productType ("product"|"auction"|"preorder"), viewedAt, productSnapshot: { title, thumb, price, storeId, storeName } }`. Items ordered newest-first (position 0 = most recent). `historyRepository.track(userSlug, item)` in a **txn**: (a) read doc; (b) filter out any existing entry with same `productId` (re-visit removes old position); (c) unshift new entry at position 0; (d) if `items.length > 50` trim tail. Silent FIFO вАФ no error, no warning (auto-tracking, not user intent). `clearForUser(userSlug)` empties items. `removeOne(userSlug, productId)` splices by productId. Constant `HISTORY_MAX = 50` in `limits.ts`. Add `history-` to CLAUDE.md Slug Prefix table (id === slug). |
| WL5 | History guest mode вАФ localStorage with same cap + merge-on-login | S | вЬЕ S44 | `useHistory()` hook: auth вЖТ POST `/api/user/history` (fire-and-forget, debounced); guest вЖТ `localStorage["letitrip:history"]` JSON array of HistoryItem (newest first, FIFO 50, same dedup-by-productId-and-unshift logic mirrored client-side). On login: `mergeGuestHistory()` reads localStorage вЖТ POSTs `/api/user/history/merge` with the array; server merges in a txn вАФ for each guest item, apply the same dedup+unshift+trim sequence (newest viewedAt wins on dedup). Clears localStorage on 2xx. |
| WL6 | History tracker integration + `/user/history` page | M | вЬЕ S44 | Call `useHistory().track({productId, productType, snapshot})` on mount of `ProductDetailPageView`, `AuctionDetailPageView`, `PreOrderDetailPageView`. Debounce 1.5s (avoid bot/back-button spam). Session-scoped `Set<productId>` de-dups within a single page session. **New page** `/user/history`: SlottedListingView, no infinite scroll needed (single doc, вЙ§50 items), filter chips (All / Products / Auctions / Pre-orders), sort fixed `viewedAt desc`. Per-card "Remove" вЖТ `DELETE /api/user/history/[productId]`. Top "Clear all" вЖТ confirm modal вЖТ `DELETE /api/user/history`. Each card shows relative timestamp ("Visited 2 hours ago"). Empty state: "Nothing here yet вАФ products you view will appear here." Nav entry under User dashboard group. `ROUTES.USER.HISTORY`. |
| WL7 | Cart 50-distinct-items cap вАФ block on overflow + toast | S | вЬЕ S44 | Server: `POST /api/cart/items` counts distinct items; if `>=50` **AND** new productId is not already in cart, return `409 { error:"CART_FULL", limit:50, current:50 }`. Per-item quantity increment is **unrestricted**. Constant `CART_MAX_ITEMS = 50` in `limits.ts`. Guest cart util (`appkit/src/features/cart/guestCart.ts`): same enforcement, same error code. Client toast variant=warning "Cart full (50/50). Remove items to add new ones." Persistent banner on `/cart` at cap. "Add to cart" buttons disabled + tooltip when cap reached. |
| WL8 | Seed + admin views + CLAUDE.md updates | M | вЬЕ S44 | (1) `appkit/src/seed/history-seed-data.ts` вАФ 10 docs (one per buyer), each with 5вАУ30 HistoryItems across mixed productTypes, viewedAt spread over last 7 days, ordered newest-first. Wire into seed route (load/delete/count) + SeedPanel meta (slugPattern `history-{userSlug}`, no media, no PII). (2) Rebuild wishlist seed as 10 one-doc-per-user docs (`wishlist-{userSlug}`) with 1вАУ15 WishlistItems each. (3) `AdminWishlistsView` (LL15): switch to top-level `wishlistRepository.findAll()` returning user-level rows (user, item count, last updatedAt) вАФ drop `collectionGroup`; clicking a row opens a SideDrawer listing that user's items. (4) New `AdminHistoryView` read-only (similar pattern): rows = user + item count + last visit; row click вЖТ SideDrawer with HistoryItems. Nav: System group. API: `GET /api/admin/history`. (5) **No composite indexes needed** (single-doc reads) вАФ only the `firestore.rules` need allow-list updates for the two new collections. (6) Update CLAUDE.md: Collection Inventory rows for `wishlists` (new shape: one-doc-per-user, items[]) and `history` (new collection); add `wishlist-` and `history-` to Slug Prefix table (note: id === slug, like products/stores). |

## Tier GP вАФ Grouped Listings *(standard products + pre-orders only; no auctions)*

> A "group" is a parent product linked to 1вАУN child products (e.g., "Human Toy Complete Set" links to "head", "legs", "arms" as separate fully independent listings). Depth is exactly 1 вАФ no grandchildren. Each member has its own title, slug, price, images, and checkout flow. The group thread is visible as a collapsible "Show group (N items)" panel on every member's detail page.

| # | Task | Complexity | Status | Part | Notes |
|---|------|-----------|--------|------|-------|
| GP1 | Grouped listings schema + `ShowGroupSection` component | M | вЬЕ | | **Schema** (`appkit/src/features/products/schemas/firestore.ts`): add to `ProductDocument`: `groupId?: string` (= parent slug; same on parent + all children), `isGroupParent?: boolean`, `groupParentSlug?: string` (null on parent; parent's slug on children), `groupChildSlugs?: string[]` (parent only), `groupTitle?: string` (e.g. "Human Toy Complete Set"). Slug convention: parent = `product-human-toy`; children append part name (`product-human-toy-head`). **New component** `appkit/src/features/products/components/ShowGroupSection.tsx` вАФ receives `groupId` + `currentSlug` + `isParent` props; renders nothing if `groupId` absent. Fetches all products/pre-orders with matching `groupId`. **Parent view**: collapsible panel "Parts in this group (N)". **Child view**: collapsible panel "Part of: [groupTitle]". Both collapsed by default. **Card style**: small circular thumbnail cards (~64 px) in a `HorizontalScroller`; cards are selectable вАФ clicking navigates to that member's detail page; current product has a highlighted ring border. Parent card shown first with a "Set" badge. **"View whole group вЖТ" button** opens a `Modal` (or `SideDrawer` if вЙ• 5 parts) with a table вАФ columns: thumbnail (click to expand image preview), name, price, condition, "View" link. Standard products + pre-orders only. **Placement**: injected via a new `renderGroupSection` render prop on `ProductDetailView` and the pre-order equivalent вАФ rendered between the buy-box/actions area and the TABS row (NOT in `belowFold`). `npx tsc --noEmit` вЖТ 0 errors. |
| GP2 | Edit-screen "Group settings" panel + inline child creation + link-existing | M | вЬЕ | | Depends on GP1. Add collapsible **"Group settings"** section to `AdminProductEditorView` and seller `ProductForm.tsx`. Hidden on auction forms. **Three states**: *(1) Not in a group* вАФ "Start a group" button вЖТ sets `isGroupParent: true`, `groupId: this.slug`. *(2) This is the group parent* вАФ shows `groupTitle` input; lists children (thumbnail, title, price, condition, "Unlink" button in batch write); **"Add child listing"** button вЖТ modal with **two tabs**: **Tab 1 вАФ Create new child**: minimal form with only the fields that differ (title, slug auto-suggested as `parent-slug-[part]`, price, short description, condition, images via MediaUploadField); all other fields (category, brand, storeId, tags, shippingInfo, returnPolicy) shown as read-only "Inherited from parent" badges; on save: creates new product doc with inherited fields + minimal changes; updates parent `groupChildSlugs` atomically; toast; "Need more control? Edit the full listing after saving" note. **Tab 2 вАФ Link existing**: searchable `DynamicSelect` across products + pre-orders by title or slug; validates: candidate not already in a group, not an auction; on confirm: batch-writes `groupId`/`groupParentSlug` onto the linked listing + adds its slug to parent `groupChildSlugs`. Also: "Dissolve group" button (confirm required) вЖТ batch-clears all group fields on parent + all children. *(3) This is a child* вАФ "Part of: [groupTitle]" read-only banner with link to parent edit page; "Leave group" button (confirm). All multi-doc writes are atomic batch. |

## Tier SC вАФ Sub-listing Categories *(all listing types: products, auctions, pre-orders)*

> A "sub-listing category" is a named bucket (e.g., "Base Set 1 Charizard 108/120") that groups multiple independent listings of the same real-world collectible with different conditions, grades, prices, and sellers. Each listing is still its own full product/auction/pre-order вАФ the sub-listing category is just the thread linking them. The public page shows all members. The detail page shows a collapsible horizontal scroller "More listings in: [name]".

| # | Task | Complexity | Status | Part | Notes |
|---|------|-----------|--------|------|-------|

## Tier SR вАФ Global Search Redesign

> Replace the tab-based `/search/[query]/tab/[tab]/sort/[sortKey]/page/[page]` flow with direct resource-type navigation. The search bar gets an inline resource type selector; submitting navigates to that resource's own public listing page with `?q=` pre-filled. Zero fuzzy search, zero third-party dependency вАФ all suggestions come from existing Firestore data.

## Tier ARCH вАФ Store Identity Architecture *(storeId/storeName public; sellerId = internal auth only)*

> **Core rule**: The store is the public identity on LetiTrip вАФ not the individual seller user behind it. Public-facing APIs, UI cards, detail pages, cart items, and profiles must show `storeId` / `storeName` / `storeSlug`. The Firebase UID of the store owner (`sellerId` internally) is an auth/internal field only вАФ it must never appear in a public API response or client-rendered prop. Admin views may additionally display `ownerId` (display alias for `sellerId` in admin context). Server-only code (checkout, analytics, payout calculation, authorization) may continue using `sellerId` for auth logic without change.
>
> **SideDrawer vs Modal rule** (enforced from this tier forward): 0 fields вЖТ `ConfirmDeleteModal`; 1вАУ2 fields вЖТ `Modal`; 3+ fields вЖТ `SideDrawer`.
>
> **User roles** (public 3-tier): `user` (basic buyer) | `seller` (has вЙ•1 store) | `admin` (platform admin). `moderator` is an internal sub-role of admin.

| # | Task | Complexity | Status | Part | Notes |
|---|------|-----------|--------|------|-------|
| ARCH1 | Public API sanitization: strip sellerId from product/review/order public responses | M | вЬЕ | S6 2026-05-11 | New `sanitizeProductForPublic`/`sanitizeProductsForPublic` helper in `appkit/src/features/products/utils/sanitize.ts` (strips sellerId/sellerName/sellerEmail/ownerId). Wired into appkit `products/api/route.ts` GET list, appkit `products/api/[id]/route.ts` GET detail, and letitrip `src/app/api/products/route.ts` GET. Reviews + orders already had no sellerId in public responses вАФ no change. |
| ARCH2 | Cart items: sellerId/sellerName вЖТ storeId/storeName | M | вЬЕ | Session 81 | Cart/Order/Coupon/Offer/Payout schemas all migrated. Checkout two-step shipping lookup (storeIdвЖТownerIdвЖТuser). Bid guard fixed. All seed data updated. All repositories renamed (findBySellerвЖТfindByStore etc.). ProductItem type gained storeName. Both appkit and main app pass tsc --noEmit 0 errors. |

Seed data maps `sellerId` вЖТ `{storeId, storeName}` via `SELLER_STORE` lookup at export time. |
