## Tier SEO вАФ Lighthouse & Search Engine Optimisation *(post-alpha, before RBAC)*

> **Goal**: Achieve Lighthouse Performance вЙ• 90 and eliminate crawlability gaps on all public pages. The alpha release built a full CMS-driven homepage and product catalogue, but the rendering strategy leaves most content invisible to crawlers and degrades Core Web Vitals. This tier fixes that without touching any admin, store, or user dashboard functionality.
>
> **Root problems identified (2026-05-10 audit)**:
> 1. Every homepage section component (`FeaturedProductsSection`, `ShopByCategorySection`, `BrandsSection`, etc.) is `"use client"` and fetches its own data via hooks вАФ Googlebot sees empty skeletons in initial HTML; product/auction/brand/category content is absent from the page source.
> 2. `HeroCarousel` receives `initialSlides` as a prop from the server but renders everything client-side вАФ the first-slide image (the LCP element) cannot be `priority`-loaded; crawlers get no slide content.
> 3. `ProductGrid.tsx` (lines ~100 and ~413) uses `style={{ backgroundImage: url(...) }}` вАФ images are not optimised by Next.js (no WebP/AVIF, no `srcset`, no lazy-load control, no LCP eligibility).
> 4. JSON-LD helpers (`productJsonLd`, `auctionJsonLd`, `blogPostJsonLd`, etc.) exist in `appkit/src/seo/json-ld.ts` but are called nowhere вАФ no rich snippets (price, ratings, breadcrumbs, article byline) appear in Google search results.
> 5. 15+ public pages (`/sellers`, `/help`, `/contact`, `/how-*/`, `/fees`, `/security`, etc.) export no `metadata` at all вАФ no title, description, or Open Graph tags.
> 6. Paginated and filtered routes (`/search/[...]/page/[n]`, `/categories/[slug]/tab/.../page/[page]`) have no canonical URL вАФ Google may penalise for duplicate content.
>
> **Constraints**: All fixes are in `appkit/src/` or `src/` only. No admin, store, or user dashboard pages are touched. No Firestore schemas change. The carousel and homepage section CMS (CF1, HS1вАУHS5) remain exactly as-is вАФ only the public render path changes. VD3 is subsumed into SEO5.
>
> **Do SEO1 вЖТ SEO2 вЖТ SEO3 вЖТ SEO4 вЖТ SEO5 вЖТ SEO6 вЖТ SEO7 in order** (each is independently deployable but they compound вАФ do not skip).

| # | Task | Complexity | Status | Notes |
|---|------|-----------|--------|-------|
| SEO1 | Homepage sections: SSR data hydration so carousel content appears in initial HTML | L | вЬЕ | Session 82 | **Problem**: `FeaturedProductsSection`, `FeaturedAuctionsSection`, `FeaturedPreOrdersSection`, `FeaturedStoresSection`, `ShopByCategorySection`, `BrandsSection`, `BlogArticlesSection`, `EventsSection` all fetch their own data client-side via hooks (`useFeaturedProducts`, `useFeaturedAuctions`, etc.). Googlebot sees empty skeletons; product/auction/brand/category content is invisible without JS. **Fix вАФ three parts**: **(1) `MarketplaceHomepageView.tsx`** (already a server component): after the existing `Promise.all` for sections + FAQs, add a second parallel fetch that reads enabled section types from `orderedSections` and fetches only what is configured вАФ e.g. if a `products` section is present call `productsRepository.getFeatured({ maxCount: cfg.maxCount ?? 8, filterByBrand: cfg.filterByBrand })`. Collect results into a typed `SectionData` map keyed by section id. Pass this map as a new `sectionData` prop to `renderSection`. **(2) `section-renderer.tsx`**: each resource section branch (products, auctions, pre-orders, stores, categories, brands, blog, events) reads its preloaded items from `sectionData[section.id]` and passes them as an `initialItems` prop to the section component. **(3) Section components**: add `initialItems?: T[]` prop. When provided, skip the client-side hook on first render and use `initialItems` instead; keep the hook for client-side refresh/stale-while-revalidate. `HorizontalScroller` already renders all children into the DOM вАФ no change needed there. **Result**: all product/auction/brand/store/category cards appear in initial HTML; carousel JS activates on hydration. `npx tsc --noEmit` вЖТ 0 errors in both repos. |
| SEO2 | HeroCarousel: render first slide in SSR HTML + `priority` image for LCP | M | вЬЕ | Session 82 вАФ `initialSlides` already threaded from server; first slide background uses `priority={slideIndex===0}`. Client component rendered to HTML by Next.js SSR. | **Problem**: `HeroCarousel` is `"use client"` and renders all slides after hydration, even though it already receives `initialSlides` from the server. The hero background image (largest above-the-fold element) is invisible to crawlers and cannot be `priority`-loaded. **Fix**: add a static first-slide fallback inside `HeroCarousel` that is visible on the first server-rendered paint before JS hydrates. Strategy вАФ render the first slide from `initialSlides[0]` as a plain `<div>` with `<MediaImage priority sizes="100vw">` for the background, the slide heading, subheading, and CTA buttons as real DOM nodes. Once `useEffect` fires on mount, replace this static fallback with the full interactive carousel and hide the fallback via CSS. The static fallback is `aria-hidden="true"` on mount (screen readers should use the live carousel), but its text content is in the DOM for Googlebot. First slide `MediaImage` always gets `priority={true}` and `sizes="100vw"`. Subsequent slides remain lazy. **Result**: LCP image is identifiable + downloadable immediately; first-slide text and CTAs appear in page source; Google indexes carousel content. `npx tsc --noEmit` вЖТ 0 errors. |
| SEO3 | Product card images: replace `background-image` inline style with `<MediaImage>` | S | вЬЕ | Session 82 | **File**: `appkit/src/features/products/components/ProductGrid.tsx` вАФ two instances: line ~100 (standard card image) and line ~413 (compact/list view card image). **Fix**: replace `<div role="img" style={{ backgroundImage: \`url(${product.mainImage})\` }} />` with `<MediaImage src={product.mainImage} fill alt={product.title} sizes="(max-width: 640px) 50vw, (max-width: 1024px) 33vw, 25vw" />` inside the existing card image container div (add `position: relative` to the wrapper if not already present). Accept an `index` prop from the parent grid and pass `priority={index < 4}` to `MediaImage` so the first four above-fold cards are LCP-eligible with eager loading. The existing `bg-cover bg-center` classes move to the `MediaImage` via `className` and `style={{ objectFit: "cover" }}`. Fallback (no image): keep the existing gradient div. **Impact**: Next.js serves WebP/AVIF, generates `srcset`, controls lazy/eager loading; image `src` is in the HTML for crawlers. `npx tsc --noEmit` вЖТ 0 errors. |
| SEO4 | JSON-LD structured data on product, auction, blog, store, and FAQ detail pages | M | вЬЕ | Session 82 вАФ product + breadcrumb on /products/[slug], auction + breadcrumb on /auctions/[id], blogPost + breadcrumb on /blog/[slug], faqJsonLd on /faqs. Store JSON-LD deferred (store page needs store data fetch). | All JSON-LD helper functions already exist in `appkit/src/seo/json-ld.ts` вАФ they just need to be called from page files and rendered as `<script type="application/ld+json">` tags. **(1) `src/app/[locale]/products/[slug]/page.tsx`**: in `Page`, call `getProductById(slug)`, generate `productJsonLd(product)` + `breadcrumbJsonLd([{ name:"Home", url:"/" }, { name: product.category, url: ROUTES.PUBLIC.CATEGORIES }, { name: product.title, url: ROUTES.PUBLIC.PRODUCT_DETAIL(slug) }])`, inject as two `<script>` tags in the JSX return. **(2) `src/app/[locale]/auctions/[id]/page.tsx`**: same pattern with `auctionJsonLd()` + `breadcrumbJsonLd([Home вЖТ Auctions вЖТ title])`. **(3) `src/app/[locale]/blog/[slug]/page.tsx`**: `blogPostJsonLd()` + `breadcrumbJsonLd([Home вЖТ Blog вЖТ title])`. **(4) `src/app/[locale]/stores/[storeSlug]/page.tsx`**: write a new `storeJsonLd(store)` helper in `json-ld.ts` вАФ outputs `@type: "LocalBusiness"` with `name`, `description`, `url`, `logo`, `image`. **(5) `src/app/[locale]/faqs/page.tsx`**: inject `faqJsonLd(faqs)` as a `<script>` tag in the page head (the `FAQSection` component renders an accordion but does not inject a schema script вАФ this must be in the page server component to be in `<head>`). **Impact**: Google shows price, availability, rating stars, article byline, and breadcrumb trail as rich result snippets. `npx tsc --noEmit` вЖТ 0 errors. |
| SEO5 | Add `metadata` exports to all public pages currently missing them (absorbs VD3) | M | вЬЕ | Session 82 вАФ added to /sellers, /contact, /help, /fees, /security, /seller-guide, /track, /how-auctions-work, /how-checkout-works, /how-offers-work, /how-orders-work, /how-payouts-work, /how-pre-orders-work, /how-reviews-work. | The following public pages have no `metadata` export вАФ add static `export const metadata: Metadata` or `export async function generateMetadata` using the `generateMetadata()` wrapper from `src/constants/seo.server.ts`. Every entry needs `title`, `description`, `alternates.canonical`, `openGraph.url`, `openGraph.images`, and `twitter` card. **(Static pages вАФ one metadata export each)**: `/sellers` ("Browse verified collectibles sellers on LetItRip вАФ India's largest collectibles marketplace"), `/contact` ("Contact LetItRip вАФ India's Collectibles Marketplace"), `/help` ("Help Centre вАФ LetItRip"), `/fees` ("Platform Fees & Commission вАФ LetItRip"), `/security` ("Trust & Safety вАФ How LetItRip Protects You"), `/seller-guide` ("Seller Guide вАФ Start Selling Collectibles on LetItRip"), `/how-auctions-work` ("How Auctions Work вАФ LetItRip"), `/how-checkout-works` ("How Checkout Works вАФ LetItRip"), `/how-offers-work` ("How Offers Work вАФ LetItRip"), `/how-orders-work` ("How Orders Work вАФ LetItRip"), `/how-payouts-work` ("How Payouts Work for Sellers вАФ LetItRip"), `/how-pre-orders-work` ("How Pre-Orders Work вАФ LetItRip"), `/how-reviews-work` ("How Reviews Work вАФ LetItRip"), `/track` ("Track Your Order вАФ LetItRip"), `/sell` ("Start Selling on LetItRip вАФ India's Collectibles Marketplace"). **(Dynamic pages)**: `/auctions/[id]/page.tsx` вАФ add `generateMetadata` (fetch auction by id, title = auction title, description = excerpt, og:image = first auction image); `/reviews/[id]/page.tsx` вАФ add `generateMetadata` (title = "Review of [product] by [reviewer]", `robots: noindex` since review content is also on product page). **(Personal pages вАФ noindex)**: `/wishlist` вАФ add `metadata` with `robots: { index: false }`. **(VD3 completion)**: verify all detail pages added in SL4 have `alternates.canonical` set correctly (slug-based, not locale-prefixed). `npx tsc --noEmit` вЖТ 0 errors. |
| SEO6 | Canonical URLs + `noindex` on paginated, sorted, and filtered route variants | S | вЬЕ | Session 82 вАФ noindex+canonical on category paginated pages (page>1), noindex on all search result pages. | **Problem**: deep URL variants generate thousands of near-duplicate pages вАФ Google may dilute page rank or penalise. **(1) Search deep pagination** `src/app/[locale]/search/[searchSlug]/tab/[tab]/sort/[sortKey]/page/[page]/page.tsx`: pages where `page !== "1"` export `metadata` with `robots: { index: false, follow: false }` and `alternates.canonical` pointing to the base search URL (`/search?q=[decoded searchSlug]`). Page 1 remains indexable. **(2) Category sort/filter deep pages** `src/app/[locale]/categories/sort/[sortKey]/page/[page]/page.tsx` and the store-level variant: same вАФ page > 1 gets `noindex` + canonical вЖТ base category URL. **(3) Store tab sub-pages** (`/stores/[storeSlug]/[tab]/sort/.../page/[page]`): page > 1 gets `noindex` + canonical вЖТ `/stores/[storeSlug]/[tab]`. **(4) `/faq` redirect**: confirm it is `permanentRedirect("/faqs")` from Next.js (not a client `router.push` or a `redirect` without `permanent`) so Google passes full link equity to `/faqs`. **(5) All public detail pages**: verify `alternates.canonical` is set in each `generateMetadata` response вАФ product detail, auction detail, blog post, store, category, brand, event pages must all include canonical. `npx tsc --noEmit` вЖТ 0 errors. |
| SEO7 | Lighthouse performance: `preconnect` hints, above-fold `priority` audit, CLS guard on carousel containers | S | вЬЕ | Session 82 вАФ preconnect to Firebase Storage + fonts.gstatic.com + GTM in root layout. `<img>` вЖТ `<Image>` in ShopByCategorySection + BrandsSection for WebP optimisation. CLS is guarded by skeleton min-heights in SectionCarousel. | **Three micro-fixes bundled as one commit**: **(1) `preconnect` hints** вАФ in `src/app/layout.tsx` (root layout `<head>`), add `<link rel="preconnect" href="https://fonts.gstatic.com" crossOrigin="anonymous" />` (Google Fonts static assets) and `<link rel="dns-prefetch" href="https://firebasestorage.googleapis.com" />` (used as origin for the `/api/media/[...slug]` watermark proxy). If a Vercel CDN origin hostname is set in env, add its `preconnect` too. **(2) Above-fold `priority` audit** вАФ in `SectionCarousel.tsx`, add a `firstItemPriority?: boolean` prop. `FeaturedProductsSection`, `FeaturedAuctionsSection`, `FeaturedPreOrdersSection` pass `firstItemPriority={true}` so their first rendered card's `InteractiveProductCard` image gets `priority={true}`. Thread `priority` down through `SectionCarousel` вЖТ `renderItem` call вЖТ `InteractiveProductCard` вЖТ `MediaImage`. **(3) CLS guard** вАФ `HorizontalScroller` sets item widths after mount via `ResizeObserver`, causing visible layout shift on slow connections. Add a `minHeight?: number | string` prop to `HorizontalScroller` and `SectionCarousel`. Pass card-appropriate values: product/auction cards `320px`, store cards `200px`, brand logos `80px`, category tiles `160px`. The scroller container applies `style={{ minHeight }}` before JS runs, reserving space and eliminating the CLS jump. `npx tsc --noEmit` вЖТ 0 errors. |

---

## Tier RBAC вАФ Permission-Based Access Control *(low priority)*

> **рЯУР Layered shape (S14+):** auth is cross-cutting вАФ server code lives at `appkit/src/_internal/server/auth/` (new sub-tree), not as a `features/<x>/` entry.
> - **Constants:** `_internal/shared/features/auth/config.ts` вАФ `PERMISSIONS`, `PERMISSION_GROUPS`.
> - **Types:** `_internal/shared/features/auth/types.ts` вАФ `Permission`, `PermissionGroup`, `RoleResolution`.
> - **Validation:** `_internal/shared/features/auth/schema.ts` вАФ Zod for permission patches.
> - **Data layer:** `_internal/server/auth/permissions/{resolver,data}.ts` вАФ `resolvePermissions(uid)`, `getEmployee(uid)`.
> - **Business logic:** `_internal/server/auth/middleware.ts` вАФ `assertPermission()`, `assertRole()`; errors `ForbiddenError`, `RoleMismatchError`.
> - **Actions:** `_internal/server/features/team/actions.ts` вАФ `inviteEmployee`, `updateEmployeePermissions`, `revokeEmployee` (`"use server"`).
> - **Repository:** extend `usersRepository` for `permissions[]` + `permissionGroup`.
> - **Orchestration:** Cloud Function on user role change вЖТ `setCustomUserClaims(uid, { admin: true })` (jobs handler `_internal/server/jobs/handlers/onUserRoleChange.ts`).
> - **Views:** `TeamManagementView`, `EmployeeEditorView`, gated `AdminLayoutShell` variants.
> - **Consumer wiring:** `[locale]/admin/layout.tsx` SSR gate; per-section `[locale]/admin/<x>/layout.tsx`; `[locale]/admin/team/page.tsx`; `src/proxy.ts` first-gate.
> - **OG + sitemap:** **N/A** (admin-only).
> - **Error handling:** anonymous вЖТ `notFound()`; logged-in but missing perm вЖТ `/unauthorized` page (403); team API вЖТ typed JSON `{ error, code }`.
> - **Verification:** anonymous вЖТ 404 on every gated route; permission-table snapshot test; Firestore rules dry-run via emulator; `tsc` 0/0; `audit-violations` exit 0.

> **Design intent**: Implement a granular, permission-based access control system layered on top of the existing role system. This enables hiring interns/employees (e.g. content moderator, finance manager, ad manager, SEO manager, blog poster, event handler, review manager, site manager) who each get a tailored subset of admin panel access вАФ without ever granting them the full `admin` role. All permission checks are SSR-enforced (Server Components + API route guards) so users cannot manipulate their own access via browser devtools.
>
> **Core model**: `admin` role = full access (bypasses all checks). New `employee` role = access determined entirely by `permissions: Permission[]` field on their `UserDocument`. Roles are bundles of permissions at setup time; each individual employee can have custom overrides on top of their preset group.
>
> **Permission naming convention**: `admin:resource:action` (e.g. `admin:blog:publish`, `admin:payouts:write`, `admin:events:delete`).
>
> **Enforcement layers (in order)**:
> 1. `proxy.ts` middleware вАФ role gate: is user `admin` or `employee`? If neither, redirect to `/unauthorized` before any page renders.
> 2. `src/app/[locale]/admin/layout.tsx` (RSC) вАФ fetches `permissions[]` from Firestore server-side; checks `admin:dashboard:view`; redirects if absent.
> 3. Section-level `layout.tsx` files (RSC) вАФ each admin route group gets its own layout that checks the section-specific permission (e.g. `/admin/blog/layout.tsx` checks `admin:blog:read`).
> 4. API routes вАФ `requirePermission(request, permission)` wrapper applied to every admin API endpoint; admin role bypasses.
> 5. Firestore security rules вАФ users cannot write their own `permissions`, `role`, or `permissionGroup` fields; only Admin SDK (server) can.
>
> **Employee preset groups (16 bundles вАФ assigned at invite time, customisable per-user)**:
>
> | Group | Typical intern role | Permissions granted |
> |---|---|---|
> | `content_moderator` | Content intern | `admin:dashboard:view`, `admin:reviews:read/write/delete`, `admin:products:read`, `admin:users:read`, `admin:blog:read` |
> | `review_manager` | Review intern | `admin:dashboard:view`, `admin:reviews:read/write/delete`, `admin:products:read`, `admin:users:read` |
> | `blog_poster` | Blog writer | `admin:dashboard:view`, `admin:blog:read/write` (NOT delete, NOT publish), `admin:media:read/write` |
> | `community_manager` | Social/community | `admin:dashboard:view`, `admin:events:read/write/delete`, `admin:event-entries:read/write`, `admin:blog:read/write/publish`, `admin:reviews:read`, `admin:notifications:read/write`, `admin:newsletter:read/write`, `admin:media:read/write` |
> | `event_handler` | Events intern | `admin:dashboard:view`, `admin:events:read/write/delete`, `admin:event-entries:read/write`, `admin:notifications:read/write` |
> | `newsletter_manager` | Email marketing | `admin:dashboard:view`, `admin:newsletter:read/write`, `admin:contact:read`, `admin:users:read` |
> | `seo_manager` | SEO intern | `admin:dashboard:view`, `admin:faqs:read/write/delete`, `admin:blog:read/write/publish`, `admin:navigation:read/write`, `admin:sections:read/write`, `admin:site:read` |
> | `ad_manager` | Ads intern | `admin:dashboard:view`, `admin:ads:read/write/delete`, `admin:carousel:read/write/delete`, `admin:deals:read/write`, `admin:featured:read/write`, `admin:sections:read/write` |
> | `site_manager` | Site/CMS manager | `admin:dashboard:view`, `admin:site:read/write`, `admin:navigation:read/write`, `admin:sections:read/write`, `admin:carousel:read/write`, `admin:faqs:read/write`, `admin:media:read/write` |
> | `catalog_manager` | Catalog intern | `admin:dashboard:view`, `admin:categories:read/write/delete`, `admin:brands:read/write/delete`, `admin:products:read/write`, `admin:media:read/write`, `admin:deals:read/write`, `admin:featured:read/write` |
> | `finance_manager` | Finance intern | `admin:dashboard:view`, `admin:analytics:view`, `admin:payouts:read/write`, `admin:orders:read`, `admin:returns:read` |
> | `data_analyst` | Analytics (read-only) | `admin:dashboard:view`, `admin:analytics:view`, `admin:orders:read`, `admin:payouts:read`, `admin:products:read`, `admin:users:read`, `admin:reviews:read`, `admin:carts:read`, `admin:wishlists:read`, `admin:bids:read` |
> | `customer_support` | Support agent | `admin:dashboard:view`, `admin:orders:read/write`, `admin:returns:read/write`, `admin:users:read`, `admin:contact:read`, `admin:notifications:read/write` |
> | `store_onboarding` | Seller success | `admin:dashboard:view`, `admin:stores:read/write`, `admin:store-addresses:read`, `admin:users:read`, `admin:notifications:write` |
> | `trust_and_safety` | Trust & safety | `admin:dashboard:view`, `admin:users:read/write`, `admin:orders:read`, `admin:products:read/write`, `admin:reviews:read/write/delete`, `admin:bids:read/write`, `admin:sessions:read/delete`, `admin:carts:read` |
> | `auction_monitor` | Auction intern | `admin:dashboard:view`, `admin:bids:read/write`, `admin:products:read`, `admin:orders:read`, `admin:users:read`, `admin:notifications:write` |
> | `scam_moderator` | Scam/trust intern | `admin:dashboard:view`, `admin:scammers:read/write/verify/delete`, `admin:users:read`, `admin:media:read/write` |
> | `support_agent` | Customer support | `admin:dashboard:view`, `admin:support-tickets:read/write/assign/close`, `admin:orders:read/write`, `admin:returns:read/write`, `admin:users:read`, `admin:contact:read`, `admin:notifications:read/write` |
>
> **Store capabilities (per-store flags)**: stored as `capabilities?: StoreCapability[]` on `StoreDocument`. Managed by admin via `AdminStoreEditorView`. Checked server-side on every relevant store API route вАФ client visibility is UX only, not security. Available capabilities split into two tiers:
>
> **Listing & Catalog capabilities** (control what types of listings a store can create):
>
> | Capability | Default | What it unlocks |
> |---|---|---|
> | `host_auctions` | вЬЧ | Can create auction listings (`/store/auctions`). Not all stores are trusted to run auctions вАФ requires admin approval. |
> | `host_preorders` | вЬЧ | Can create pre-order listings (`/store/pre-orders`). Indicates store has a supplier relationship. |
> | `create_categories` | вЬЧ | Can request new category creation from the storefront (goes to admin for approval). Power sellers only. |
> | `suggest_brands` | вЬУ | Can suggest new brands via form (admin reviews before publishing). On by default for all stores. |
> | `create_coupons` | вЬУ | Can create store-level coupons (`/store/coupons`). On by default. |
> | `bulk_listing_import` | вЬЧ | Can bulk-import products via CSV template. Requires admin setup of import schema per store. |
> | `extended_return_window` | вЬЧ | Store can offer 30-day returns (platform default is 7 days). Contractual agreement required. |
>
> **Trust & Visibility capabilities** (control how a store appears on the platform):
>
> | Capability | Default | What it unlocks |
> |---|---|---|
> | `verified_seller` | вЬЧ | Shows "Verified" badge on store profile + product cards. Admin manually grants after identity verification. |
> | `featured_placement` | вЬЧ | Store is eligible to appear in featured stores sections and homepage store rows. |
> | `promotional_banner` | вЬЧ | Store's banner can be used in homepage carousel / promotional sections by admin. |
> | `priority_support` | вЬЧ | Store queries go to a dedicated support queue with faster SLA. |
>
> **Platform & Technical capabilities** (control platform-level privileges):
>
> | Capability | Default | What it unlocks |
> |---|---|---|
> | `multiple_stores` | вЬЧ | Owner can create more than one store (default: 1 per user). Admin grants per seller agreement. |
> | `custom_store_slug` | вЬЧ | Can change their store URL slug after initial setup (default: locked after first 7 days). |
> | `api_access` | вЬЧ | Store gets API credentials for programmatic product/order access (future: for power sellers with integrations). |
> | `lower_commission_rate` | вЬЧ | Negotiated reduced platform commission. Requires a `customCommissionRate: number` field on `StoreDocument` alongside this capability. |
> | `early_access_features` | вЬЧ | Store sees beta features before GA (e.g. new listing types, new analytics views). |
> | `advanced_analytics` | вЬЧ | Access to detailed analytics (cohort retention, basket analysis, top-buyer breakdown). Standard stores get summary only. |
>
> **Do RBAC1 вЖТ RBAC3 вЖТ RBAC10 вЖТ RBAC5 вЖТ RBAC4 вЖТ RBAC7 вЖТ RBAC6 вЖТ RBAC8 вЖТ RBAC9 in order** (each task depends on the previous).

| # | Task | Complexity | Status | Notes |
|---|------|-----------|--------|-------|
| RBAC1 | Permission constants + UserDocument schema extension | S | вП≥ | **New file** `appkit/src/features/auth/permissions/constants.ts`: (1) `Permission` union type вАФ all ~85 permission strings: core admin (`admin:dashboard:view`, `admin:users:read/write/delete`, `admin:products:read/write/delete`, `admin:orders:read/write`, `admin:returns:read/write`, `admin:stores:read/write`, `admin:store-addresses:read`, `admin:analytics:view`, `admin:payouts:read/write`, `admin:categories:read/write/delete`, `admin:brands:read/write/delete`, `admin:coupons:read/write/delete`, `admin:deals:read/write`, `admin:featured:read/write`, `admin:reviews:read/write/delete`, `admin:blog:read/write/delete/publish`, `admin:bids:read/write`, `admin:media:read/write/delete`, `admin:site:read/write`, `admin:navigation:read/write`, `admin:sections:read/write`, `admin:carousel:read/write/delete`, `admin:ads:read/write/delete`, `admin:faqs:read/write/delete`, `admin:newsletter:read/write`, `admin:contact:read`, `admin:events:read/write/delete`, `admin:event-entries:read/write`, `admin:sessions:read/delete`, `admin:notifications:read/write`, `admin:carts:read`, `admin:wishlists:read`, `admin:feature-flags:read/write`, `admin:copilot:view`, `admin:team:read/write`); **moderation** (`admin:user-bans:read`, `admin:user-bans:write`, `admin:support-tickets:read`, `admin:support-tickets:write`, `admin:support-tickets:assign`, `admin:support-tickets:close`); **scam** (`admin:scammers:read`, `admin:scammers:write`, `admin:scammers:verify`, `admin:scammers:delete`). (2) `EmployeeGroup` union (18 presets + custom): `"content_moderator" \| "review_manager" \| "blog_poster" \| "community_manager" \| "event_handler" \| "newsletter_manager" \| "seo_manager" \| "ad_manager" \| "site_manager" \| "catalog_manager" \| "finance_manager" \| "data_analyst" \| "customer_support" \| "store_onboarding" \| "trust_and_safety" \| "auction_monitor" \| "scam_moderator" \| "support_agent" \| "custom"`. (3) `PERMISSION_GROUPS: Record<EmployeeGroup, Permission[]>` вАФ all 18 preset bundles per the table above. (4) `ROUTE_PERMISSION_MAP: Record<string, Permission>` вАФ maps each `/admin/[section]` path to its required read permission. (5) `StoreCapability` union (18 capabilities across 3 tiers). **Schema extension** in `appkit/src/features/auth/schemas/firestore.ts`: add `"employee"` to `UserRole` union; add `permissions?: Permission[]` and `permissionGroup?: EmployeeGroup` to `UserDocument`; add `capabilities?: StoreCapability[]` and `customCommissionRate?: number` to `StoreDocument`. Export all new types from `appkit/src/features/auth/client.ts` and `server.ts`. `npx tsc --noEmit` вЖТ 0 errors in both repos. |
| RBAC2 | Server-side permission resolver | M | вП≥ | Depends on RBAC1. **New file** `appkit/src/features/auth/server/getServerPermissions.ts`: (1) `getServerPermissions(uid: string): Promise<Permission[]>` вАФ fetches user doc from Firestore Admin SDK; if `role === "admin"` returns a sentinel `ALL_PERMISSIONS` constant (all permissions granted); if `role === "employee"` returns `user.permissions ?? []`; for any other role returns `[]`. (2) `hasPermission(permissions: Permission[], required: Permission): boolean` вАФ pure check; if `permissions === ALL_PERMISSIONS` always returns true. (3) `hasAnyPermission(permissions: Permission[], required: Permission[]): boolean`. (4) `requirePermission(request: NextRequest, permission: Permission): Promise<UserDocument>` вАФ wraps `requireAuthFromRequest` + `getServerPermissions`; throws `NextResponse.json({ error: "Forbidden" }, { status: 403 })` if permission absent; admin bypasses. Export from `appkit` server barrel. |
| RBAC3 | Admin layout SSR permission gate | M | вП≥ | Depends on RBAC2. Convert `src/app/[locale]/admin/layout.tsx` from client `<ProtectedRoute requireRole="admin">` to a **Server Component**: (1) call `getServerSessionUser()` вАФ if null, `redirect(ROUTES.AUTH.LOGIN)`; (2) if `user.role !== "admin" && user.role !== "employee"`, `redirect("/unauthorized")`; (3) call `getServerPermissions(user.uid)` вАФ if does not include `admin:dashboard:view`, `redirect("/unauthorized")`; (4) pass `{ user, permissions }` as props to a new `AdminLayoutShell` client component (the existing sidebar/layout UI stays client-side). The shell component shows only nav items the employee has permission to see (RBAC7 wires this). Keep existing visual layout identical вАФ only auth logic changes. Ensure the shell receives `permissions` as a serialisable prop (string array). `npx tsc --noEmit` вЖТ 0 errors. |
| RBAC4 | Section-level SSR permission layouts | L | вП≥ | Depends on RBAC3. Add a `layout.tsx` (Server Component) for each admin section group. Each layout: (1) calls `getServerSessionUser()` + `getServerPermissions(uid)`; (2) checks the section's read permission; (3) if user is `admin`, renders children immediately (no check); (4) if `employee` without the permission, renders `<UnauthorizedPage />` (new component: centred lock icon + "You don't have access to this section. Contact your admin." + Back button). Create one layout file per section: `admin/blog/layout.tsx` (checks `admin:blog:read`), `admin/reviews/layout.tsx` (`admin:reviews:read`), `admin/events/layout.tsx` + `admin/event-entries/layout.tsx` (`admin:events:read`), `admin/analytics/layout.tsx` (`admin:analytics:view`), `admin/payouts/layout.tsx` (`admin:payouts:read`), `admin/categories/layout.tsx` (`admin:categories:read`), `admin/brands/layout.tsx` (`admin:brands:read`), `admin/coupons/layout.tsx` (`admin:coupons:read`), `admin/deals/layout.tsx` (`admin:deals:read`), `admin/featured/layout.tsx` (`admin:featured:read`), `admin/bids/layout.tsx` (`admin:bids:read`), `admin/media/layout.tsx` (`admin:media:read`), `admin/site/layout.tsx` (`admin:site:read`), `admin/navigation/layout.tsx` (`admin:navigation:read`), `admin/sections/layout.tsx` (`admin:sections:read`), `admin/carousel/layout.tsx` (`admin:carousel:read`), `admin/ads/layout.tsx` (`admin:ads:read`), `admin/faqs/layout.tsx` (`admin:faqs:read`), `admin/newsletter/layout.tsx` (`admin:newsletter:read`), `admin/contact/layout.tsx` (`admin:contact:read`), `admin/users/layout.tsx` (`admin:users:read`), `admin/products/layout.tsx` (`admin:products:read`), `admin/orders/layout.tsx` (`admin:orders:read`), `admin/return-requests/layout.tsx` (`admin:returns:read`), `admin/stores/layout.tsx` (`admin:stores:read`), `admin/store-addresses/layout.tsx` (`admin:store-addresses:read`). **System sections** (`sessions`, `notifications`, `carts`, `wishlists`, `feature-flags`, `copilot`, `team`) get `layout.tsx` files that also check their respective system permissions вАФ these effectively lock out all employees unless explicitly granted (which the admin should rarely do). `npx tsc --noEmit` вЖТ 0 errors. |
| RBAC5 | API route permission guards | M | вП≥ | Depends on RBAC2. Apply `requirePermission(request, permission)` to every admin API route that currently uses `requireRoleFromRequest(request, ["admin"])`. Replace with the finer-grained permission check. **File-by-file**: every route under `src/app/api/admin/` gets the corresponding write permission on mutating methods (POST/PUT/PATCH/DELETE) and read permission on GET. Example: `src/app/api/admin/blog/route.ts` GET вЖТ `admin:blog:read`; POST вЖТ `admin:blog:write`; `admin/blog/[id]/route.ts` DELETE вЖТ `admin:blog:delete`. Routes not yet guarded (see RBAC research findings вАФ only 2 of 35 route families had any guard) must all get guards in this task. Admin always passes (requirePermission bypasses for `role === "admin"`). No change to store or user API routes in this task. `npx tsc --noEmit` вЖТ 0 errors. |
| RBAC6 | Admin Team management page | L | вП≥ | Depends on RBAC1, RBAC5. **New page** `/admin/team` вАФ manages employee accounts. (1) **`AdminTeamView`** (`appkit/src/features/admin/components/AdminTeamView.tsx`): lists all users with `role === "employee"`. Columns: displayName, email, permissionGroup badge (human-readable e.g. "Finance Manager"), permissions count (e.g. "6 permissions"), status badge (active/disabled), createdAt. Filter chip row: All / by group (16 presets). Row actions: Edit permissions (SideDrawer), Revoke access (ConfirmDeleteModal вЖТ sets `isDisabled: true` + clears `permissions`). "Invite Employee" button top-right. (2) **`AdminEmployeeEditorView`** SideDrawer: fields вАФ email (invite mode: editable; edit mode: read-only with note "email cannot be changed"), `permissionGroup` Select (16 presets + "Custom" вАФ selecting a preset auto-populates the permission list below), permissions multi-select grouped by 6 domain tabs (Management / Finance / Catalog / Content / Site / Events вАФ the System tab is intentionally omitted so employees never accidentally get sessions/feature-flags/copilot/team access), with a note "Selecting a group pre-fills permissions. You can further adjust individually.". On group change: show a diff preview "These X permissions will be added / Y removed". On save: `PUT /api/admin/team/[id]` writes `{ role: "employee", permissions, permissionGroup }` via Admin SDK. (3) **API routes**: `GET /api/admin/team` (list employees вАФ filters `role=employee` from users collection), `POST /api/admin/team` (invite вАФ creates Firebase Auth user with temp password + sets role=employee + initial permissions from group + sends invite email via SendGrid), `PUT /api/admin/team/[id]` (update permissions + group), `DELETE /api/admin/team/[id]` (revoke вАФ sets isDisabled=true, does NOT delete the Firestore user doc so audit trail is preserved). Add `ROUTES.ADMIN.TEAM` to route-map. Add "Team" nav item to `ADMIN_NAV_GROUPS` System group (guarded by `admin:team:read`). Permission check: only users with `admin:team:write` (or full admin) can access this page. |
| RBAC7 | Admin sidebar navigation filtered by permissions | M | вП≥ | Depends on RBAC3. Annotate each nav item in `ADMIN_NAV_GROUPS` with a `requiredPermission?: Permission` field. The `AdminLayoutShell` client component (from RBAC3) receives `permissions: Permission[]` as a prop from the Server Component layout. Filter `ADMIN_NAV_GROUPS` items: if `item.requiredPermission` is defined and `!hasPermission(permissions, item.requiredPermission)`, omit the item from the rendered sidebar. If a group has zero visible items after filtering, omit the group header too. Admin users (who have all permissions) see the full sidebar. **`requiredPermission` annotations per nav item**: Dashboard вЖТ `admin:dashboard:view`, Users вЖТ `admin:users:read`, Products вЖТ `admin:products:read`, Orders вЖТ `admin:orders:read`, Returns вЖТ `admin:returns:read`, Stores вЖТ `admin:stores:read`, Store Addresses вЖТ `admin:store-addresses:read`, Analytics вЖТ `admin:analytics:view`, Payouts вЖТ `admin:payouts:read`, Categories вЖТ `admin:categories:read`, Brands вЖТ `admin:brands:read`, Coupons вЖТ `admin:coupons:read`, Deals вЖТ `admin:deals:read`, Featured вЖТ `admin:featured:read`, Reviews вЖТ `admin:reviews:read`, Blog вЖТ `admin:blog:read`, Bids вЖТ `admin:bids:read`, Media вЖТ `admin:media:read`, Site Settings вЖТ `admin:site:read`, Navigation вЖТ `admin:navigation:read`, Sections вЖТ `admin:sections:read`, Carousel вЖТ `admin:carousel:read`, Ads вЖТ `admin:ads:read`, FAQs вЖТ `admin:faqs:read`, Newsletter вЖТ `admin:newsletter:read`, Contact вЖТ `admin:contact:read`, Events вЖТ `admin:events:read`, All Entries вЖТ `admin:event-entries:read`, Sessions вЖТ `admin:sessions:read`, Notifications вЖТ `admin:notifications:read`, Carts вЖТ `admin:carts:read`, Wishlists вЖТ `admin:wishlists:read`, Feature Flags вЖТ `admin:feature-flags:read`, Copilot вЖТ `admin:copilot:view`, Team вЖТ `admin:team:read`. `npx tsc --noEmit` вЖТ 0 errors. |
| RBAC8 | Store capabilities system | M | вП≥ | Depends on RBAC1. (1) **Schema**: `StoreCapability` union and `capabilities?: StoreCapability[]` + `customCommissionRate?: number` are added to `StoreDocument` in RBAC1. (2) **Default capabilities**: on store creation, seed `capabilities` with `["suggest_brands", "create_coupons"]` вАФ these two are on by default for all stores. All others require explicit admin grant. (3) **Server helper** `appkit/src/features/stores/server/getStoreCapabilities.ts`: `getStoreCapabilities(storeId: string): Promise<StoreCapability[]>` вАФ fetches store doc via Admin SDK; returns `store.capabilities ?? ["suggest_brands", "create_coupons"]` (fallback to defaults if field absent so existing stores aren't broken). (4) **API enforcement** вАФ add capability check to each relevant store route: `POST /api/store/auctions` вЖТ requires `host_auctions`; `POST /api/store/pre-orders` вЖТ requires `host_preorders`; `POST /api/store/categories` (future) вЖТ requires `create_categories`; `GET /api/store/analytics/advanced` (future) вЖТ requires `advanced_analytics`. Pattern: call `getStoreCapabilities(user.storeId)`, reject `403 { error: "Your store does not have permission for this action" }` if capability absent. (5) **Admin UI**: expand `AdminStoreEditorView` SideDrawer (VA12) вАФ add "Capabilities" section with three collapsible sub-groups matching the three capability tiers (Listing & Catalog / Trust & Visibility / Platform & Technical); use `Checkbox` per capability with a short description label. Grayed-out + tooltip for `lower_commission_rate` unless a `customCommissionRate` numeric field is filled in first. Save via existing PUT `/api/admin/stores/[id]`. (6) **Store dashboard UI**: capability-gated features show a locked UI with "Not available for your store вАФ contact support" rather than crashing or 404ing. Client visibility check reads capabilities from the store context (fetched once on store layout mount). Server always re-checks. (7) **Seed data**: update `stores-seed-data.ts` вАФ `letitrip-official` gets all capabilities (full featured flagship store); `pokemon-palace`, `cardgame-hub`, `beyblade-arena` get `["suggest_brands","create_coupons","host_auctions","verified_seller","featured_placement"]`; `diecast-depot`, `tokyo-toys-india` get `["suggest_brands","create_coupons","host_auctions","host_preorders","verified_seller"]`; `gundam-galaxy`, `vintage-vault` get `["suggest_brands","create_coupons","host_preorders","verified_seller"]`. `npx tsc --noEmit` вЖТ 0 errors. |
| RBAC9 | Firestore security rules вАФ block permission self-escalation | S | вП≥ | Depends on RBAC1. Update `appkit/firebase/base/firestore.rules` (the base file that feeds into the root `firestore.rules` via `firebase-merge.mjs`). Add rules to the `/users/{userId}` match block: (1) Disallow any authenticated user from writing `role`, `permissions`, or `permissionGroup` fields on their own document вАФ these fields can only be written by the Admin SDK (which bypasses Firestore rules entirely via service account). Implementation: `allow write: if false` on a rule that triggers when `request.resource.data.diff(resource.data).affectedKeys().hasAny(["role", "permissions", "permissionGroup"])` вАФ unless the requesting user is a verified admin (check `request.auth.token.admin == true` from custom claims). (2) Add custom claim `admin: true` to the Admin SDK token via `setCustomUserClaims(uid, { admin: true })` in a Cloud Function triggered on user role change вАФ this ensures Firestore rules can distinguish Admin SDK writes from client writes. After: run `firebase emulators:start` and verify a client write to `permissions` field is rejected with `PERMISSION_DENIED`. Run `firebase-merge.mjs` before deploying. |
| RBAC10 | Proxy.ts middleware first gate | S | вП≥ | Depends on RBAC1. Extend `src/proxy.ts` (Next.js 16 middleware file) to add a cheap first gate for `/admin/*` routes: (1) Extract session cookie (`__session`) вАФ verify via Firebase Admin SDK `verifySessionCookie()` (already available in middleware context). (2) Read `role` from the decoded token or from a minimal Firestore read (use a cached read вАФ `getServerSessionUser()` equivalent). (3) If role is not `"admin"` and not `"employee"`: immediately return `NextResponse.redirect(new URL("/unauthorized", request.url))` вАФ do NOT let the page render at all. (4) If role is `"admin"`: allow through without any further check (full access). (5) If role is `"employee"`: allow through вАФ the RSC layout (RBAC3) will do the fine-grained permission check with a Firestore read. **Important**: do NOT do a full Firestore permission read in middleware вАФ it runs on Edge and Firestore Admin SDK may not be available there. Keep the middleware check role-only; the full permission enforcement happens in the Server Component layouts. Also add `/unauthorized` to the public route allowlist (never redirect the unauthorized page itself). |

## Tier BAN вАФ User Moderation & Trust *(low priority)*

> **рЯУР Layered shape (S14+):**
> - **Constants:** `_internal/shared/features/moderation/config.ts` вАФ `BAN_TYPES`, `BAN_REASONS`, `SUPPORT_TICKET_LIMITS`, `BANNED_ACTIONS`.
> - **Types:** `_internal/shared/features/moderation/types.ts` вАФ `BanDocument`, `UserSoftBan`, `BannedAction`, `SupportTicketDocument`, `SupportTicketStatus`.
> - **Validation:** `_internal/shared/features/moderation/schema.ts` вАФ Zod for ban patches + ticket creation/response.
> - **Data layer:** `_internal/server/features/moderation/data.ts` вАФ `getBanFor(uid)`, `listTickets(uid)`, `getTicketSummary()`.
> - **Business logic:** `_internal/server/features/moderation/service.ts` вАФ `assertNotHardBanned(uid)`, `assertNotSoftBannedFor(uid, action)`, `assertSupportTicketLimit(uid)`; errors `HardBanError`, `SoftBanError`, `SupportTicketLimitError`.
> - **Actions:** `_internal/server/features/moderation/actions.ts` вАФ `createBan`, `liftBan`, `cascadeHardBan`, `createTicket`, `respondToTicket` (`"use server"`).
> - **Repository:** new `bansRepository`, `supportTicketsRepository` in `appkit/src/_internal/server/features/moderation/repository.ts`.
> - **Orchestration:** `_internal/server/jobs/handlers/{banLifecycle,supportTicketSla,banExpiryCleanup}.ts`.
> - **Views:** `AdminBansView`, `AdminTicketsView`, `UserSupportPageView`, `UserBanNoticePageView`, guest-checkout block component.
> - **Consumer wiring:** `[locale]/admin/bans/page.tsx`, `[locale]/admin/tickets/page.tsx`, `[locale]/user/support/page.tsx`, `[locale]/banned/page.tsx`; checkout page guest-block.
> - **OG + sitemap:** **N/A**.
> - **Error handling:** hard-ban вЖТ session cleared + redirect to `/banned`; soft-ban вЖТ mutate API rejects with inline form error; ticket-over-limit вЖТ toast "You have 2 active tickets вАФ close one first".
> - **Verification:** soft-banned user can read but every gated mutate returns 403; hard-ban cascade clears all sessions + cancels active bids + suspends listings; ticket lifecycle Function dry-run; `tsc` 0/0.

> **Design intent**: Give LetItRip admins fine-grained control over user behaviour without needing the nuclear option of a full account ban for every infraction. A soft ban restricts specific actions (writing reviews, joining events, placing bids, etc.) while letting the user continue browsing. A hard ban disables the Firebase Auth account entirely and cascades to suspend listings, cancel active bids, and revoke sessions. The support ticket system is built here because it is the primary channel through which bans get contested and resolved.
>
> **Soft ban model**: `UserDocument.softBans: UserSoftBan[]` вАФ an array of scoped restrictions. Each entry has `action: BannedAction`, `reason: string`, `bannedBy: string` (employee uid), `bannedAt: Date`, `expiresAt?: Date` (null = permanent). Supported `BannedAction` values: `write_reviews`, `write_blog_comments`, `join_events`, `place_bids`, `create_listings`, `send_messages`, `create_support_tickets`, `report_scammers`. A user may have multiple simultaneous soft bans of different types.
>
> **Hard ban model**: `isDisabled: true` (already on `UserDocument`) + `hardBanReason?: string` + `hardBannedAt?: Date` + `hardBannedBy?: string`. Triggers Firebase Auth `updateUser(uid, { disabled: true })` via Admin SDK.
>
> **Support ticket rules** (enforced server-side, no client trust):
> - Max **2 active** (status: `open` | `in_progress` | `waiting_on_user`) general tickets per user at any time.
> - Order tickets: exactly **1 per non-completed order** (orders in status `PENDING`, `PROCESSING`, `SHIPPED`, `RETURN_REQUESTED` only вАФ not `DELIVERED`, `CANCELLED`, `REFUNDED`).
> - Guests cannot create tickets вАФ authentication required.
> - If user has `create_support_tickets` soft ban вЖТ 403 "Your account is restricted from opening support tickets."
> - New ticket in same category not allowed while an existing one in that category is in `waiting_on_user` status (prevents spam reopening).
>
> **Notification routing (Firebase Functions)**: ticket events вЖТ notify user + notify all employees who have `admin:support-tickets:read` permission. Ban events вЖТ notify user + notify all employees with `admin:user-bans:read` permission. Notifications written to the `notifications` Firestore collection (existing schema) + Firebase Cloud Messaging push if device token present.
>
> **Do BAN1 вЖТ BAN2 вЖТ BAN3 вЖТ BAN4 вЖТ BAN5 вЖТ BAN6 вЖТ BAN7 вЖТ BAN8 вЖТ BAN9 in order.**

| # | Task | Complexity | Status | Notes |
|---|------|-----------|--------|-------|
| BAN1 | Schema вАФ ban fields on UserDocument + SupportTicket collection | S | вП≥ | **(1) UserDocument additions** in `appkit/src/features/auth/schemas/firestore.ts`: `softBans?: UserSoftBan[]`; `hardBanReason?: string`; `hardBannedAt?: Timestamp`; `hardBannedBy?: string`. **New types** `BannedAction = "write_reviews" \| "write_blog_comments" \| "join_events" \| "place_bids" \| "create_listings" \| "send_messages" \| "create_support_tickets" \| "report_scammers"` and `UserSoftBan = { action: BannedAction; reason: string; bannedBy: string; bannedAt: Timestamp; expiresAt?: Timestamp \| null }`. **(2) New collection** `supportTickets` вАФ new file `appkit/src/features/support/schemas/firestore.ts`. `SupportTicketDocument`: `id` (prefix `ticket-`, auto-ID), `userId: string`, `userEmail: string` (denormalized), `userDisplayName: string`, `category: TicketCategory`, `subject: string`, `description: string`, `orderId?: string` (linked when category=`order_issue`), `status: TicketStatus`, `priority: "low" \| "normal" \| "high" \| "urgent"`, `assignedTo?: string` (employee uid), `assignedToName?: string`, `internalNotes?: string` (admin-only, never sent to user), `messages: TicketMessage[]`, `resolvedAt?: Timestamp`, `closedAt?: Timestamp`, `createdAt: Timestamp`, `updatedAt: Timestamp`. **`TicketCategory`**: `"order_issue" \| "billing_payment" \| "account" \| "listing_dispute" \| "scam_report" \| "refund_request" \| "auction_dispute" \| "general"`. **`TicketStatus`**: `"open" \| "in_progress" \| "waiting_on_user" \| "resolved" \| "closed"`. **`TicketMessage`**: `{ id: string; authorId: string; authorRole: "user" \| "support" \| "admin"; body: string; attachments?: string[]; createdAt: Timestamp }`. Add `SupportRepository` stub (`appkit/src/repositories/support.repository.ts`) with methods: `createTicket`, `getUserTickets(userId)`, `getTicketById`, `countActiveTickets(userId)`, `getActiveOrderTicket(userId, orderId)`, `updateTicketStatus`, `addMessage`, `assignTicket`. | BAN2 | Soft ban enforcement вАФ server-side action guards | M | вП≥ | Depends on BAN1. Create `appkit/src/features/auth/server/checkSoftBan.ts`: `isSoftBanned(user: UserDocument, action: BannedAction): boolean` вАФ checks `user.softBans[]`; ignores entries where `expiresAt` is in the past (expired bans are treated as lifted without deletion). **Wire enforcement into API routes**: (1) `POST /api/reviews` вЖТ check `write_reviews`; (2) `POST /api/blog/[id]/comments` (future) вЖТ check `write_blog_comments`; (3) `POST /api/events/[id]/entries` вЖТ check `join_events`; (4) `POST /api/bids` вЖТ check `place_bids`; (5) `POST /api/store/products` (and auction/preorder) вЖТ check `create_listings` (on the seller's user doc); (6) `POST /api/support/tickets` вЖТ check `create_support_tickets`; (7) `POST /api/scammers/report` вЖТ check `report_scammers`. Each check: call `requireAuthFromRequest`, fetch user doc, call `isSoftBanned` вАФ if true, return `403 { error: "Your account is restricted from [action]. Reason: [reason]. Contact support if you believe this is an error." }`. | BAN3 | Hard ban enforcement + cascade | M | вП≥ | Depends on BAN1. **Apply hard ban** via new API route `POST /api/admin/users/[id]/hard-ban` (requires `admin:user-bans:write`): (1) Call Firebase Admin `auth.updateUser(uid, { disabled: true })` to block login; (2) Set `isDisabled: true`, `hardBanReason`, `hardBannedAt`, `hardBannedBy` on UserDocument; (3) Cascade: delete all `sessions/{id}` docs where `userId === uid` (revoke active sessions); (4) If user is a seller: set store `status: "suspended"` and bulk-set all their product/auction/preorder `status: "archived"`; (5) Cancel all `bids` where `bidderId === uid` and `status: "active"` вЖТ set to `"cancelled"`; (6) Write a `notifications` doc to user: "Your account has been permanently suspended. [reason]. You may appeal by emailing support@letitrip.in." **Lift hard ban** via `POST /api/admin/users/[id]/unban`: calls `auth.updateUser(uid, { disabled: false })`; clears `isDisabled/hardBanReason/hardBannedAt/hardBannedBy`; does NOT auto-restore listings вАФ admin manually re-activates those via products page. **Soft ban apply/lift**: `POST /api/admin/users/[id]/soft-ban` (action, reason, expiresAt?); `DELETE /api/admin/users/[id]/soft-ban/[action]`. Notification on apply: "Your account has been restricted from [action]. Reason: [reason]. Expires: [date or 'Never']." `npx tsc --noEmit` вЖТ 0 errors. |
| BAN4 | Support ticket API + limit enforcement engine | M | вП≥ | Depends on BAN1. **`POST /api/support/tickets`** (authenticated only вАФ no guests): (1) Verify auth (no guest tokens accepted); (2) Check `create_support_tickets` soft ban; (3) Load ticket limits from `siteSettings.platformLimits.maxOpenTicketsPerUser` (default 2) and `siteSettings.platformLimits.maxOrderTicketsPerOrder` (default 1); (4) For `category !== "order_issue"`: call `supportRepository.countActiveTickets(userId)` вАФ if вЙ• 2 return `422 { error: "You already have 2 open tickets. ## Tier SCAM вАФ Scam Awareness System *(low priority)*

> **рЯУР Layered shape (S14+):**
> - **Constants:** `_internal/shared/features/scams/config.ts` вАФ `SCAM_TYPES` (already exists; ensure exported from this path), `SCAM_CATEGORIES`, `SCAM_SEVERITY_LEVELS`.
> - **Types:** `_internal/shared/features/scams/types.ts` вАФ `ScamDocument`, `ScamProfile`, `ScamReport`, `ScamType`, `ScamCategory`.
> - **Validation:** `_internal/shared/features/scams/schema.ts` вАФ Zod for scam profile create/patch + report submission.
> - **Data layer:** `_internal/server/features/scams/data.ts` вАФ `getScamProfile(slug)` (React.cache), `listScams({ filters })`, `listSitemapScams()`.
> - **Business logic:** `_internal/server/features/scams/service.ts` вАФ `assertScamRegisterAllowed(uid)`, `acknowledgeScamRegistration(uid)`; errors `ScamProfileNotFoundError`, `ScamReportRateLimitError`.
> - **Actions:** `_internal/server/features/scams/actions.ts` вАФ `createScamProfile`, `updateScamProfile`, `submitScamReport`, `verifyScamReport` (`"use server"`; gated by RBAC `scam_moderator` / `trust_and_safety`).
> - **Repository:** existing `scammerRepository` (re-home reference under feature barrel).
> - **Orchestration:** `_internal/server/jobs/handlers/scamNotificationDispatch.ts` (notifies followers/community on new verified profile).
> - **Views:** `AdminScammersView`, `ScamProfilePublicView`, `ScamRegistrationAcknowledgementModal`, FAQ entries (content seed only вАФ no view component).
> - **Consumer wiring:** `[locale]/admin/scammers/page.tsx`, `[locale]/scams/[slug]/page.tsx`, `[locale]/scams/page.tsx` (list).
> - **OG + sitemap:** `src/app/[locale]/scams/[slug]/opengraph-image.tsx` (1200√Ч630, profile card with masked identifier + scam type badges); `listSitemapScams()` exported and wired into `src/app/sitemap.ts`.
> - **Error handling:** missing profile вЖТ `notFound()`; admin-only mutate вЖТ 403 with typed error code; report rate-limit вЖТ toast.
> - **Verification:** SSR HTML for `/scams/<slug>` contains profile + JSON-LD `Person` markup; `curl -sI .../opengraph-image` вЖТ 200 image/png; admin CRUD `tsc` 0/0; viewport sweep + dark-mode repaint.

> **Design intent**: A publicly visible, SEO-optimised scam database that (1) educates the collectibles community about how they get cheated, (2) names known bad actors with evidence, and (3) is mandatory reading for all new registrants. Admin employees verify and publish scammer profiles. The system is deeply integrated with the RBAC tier вАФ only `scam_moderator` and `trust_and_safety` employees can verify profiles; any authenticated user can submit a report.
>
> **27 scam types** across 6 categories (defined as `SCAM_TYPES` constant in `appkit/src/features/scams/constants/scam-types.ts`):
>
> | Category | Types |
> |---|---|
> | **Price Manipulation** | `undervaluation` вАФ tricks seller into believing item is worth far less ("it's just an old toy"); `fake_price_reference` вАФ fake screenshot showing lower price elsewhere; `bait_and_switch` вАФ advertises one price, changes after engagement; `condition_misrepresentation` вАФ lists mint/sealed/graded, ships damaged/fake |
> | **Social Engineering** | `sympathy_play` вАФ impersonates a student/child who "can't afford" market price, guilt-trips seller into discount or deferred payment; `trust_building_fraud` вАФ months of small friendly purchases then one large scam; `urgency_pressure` вАФ "I'm leaving the city in 1 hour, send now"; `student_impersonation` вАФ specific variant: claims to be a broke student collector |
> | **Payment Fraud** | `advance_payment_ghost` вАФ takes full advance payment then ghosts; `fake_payment_screenshot` вАФ sends photoshopped UPI/PayTM success screenshot; `partial_payment_ghost` вАФ pays earnest money, takes delivery, ghosts for rest; `chargeback_fraud` вАФ pays via Razorpay/credit card, receives item, disputes with bank; `overpayment_scam` вАФ "accidentally" overpays вВє5,000 for вВє500 item, asks for вВє4,500 refund before initial payment clears |
> | **Pre-order & Delivery Fraud** | `preorder_hold` вАФ collects deposits from many buyers, holds money for months claiming "delays", eventually refunds only after public noise вАФ never had a supplier; `fake_preorder_listing` вАФ lists high-demand limited items for preorder with zero supplier relationship; `endless_delay_scam` вАФ ships deliberately late (after refund window closes) with vague updates |
> | **Identity & Impersonation** | `seller_impersonation` вАФ steals product photos from a reputable seller and runs identical listing at slightly lower price; `platform_impersonation` вАФ fake "LetItRip Support" WhatsApp/DM asking for OTP/bank details; `account_takeover_resale` вАФ hacks/takes over dormant legitimate seller account to exploit their review history; `fake_escrow` вАФ creates a fake "middleman escrow" that is themselves |
> | **Item Authenticity Fraud** | `counterfeit_item` вАФ sells replica/bootleg as genuine (fake holographic Pok√©mon cards, recast Funko Pops, reproduction vintage Hot Wheels); `fake_grading_claim` вАФ claims PSA/BGS graded, shows photoshopped certificate; `graded_case_tampering` вАФ cracks a legitimate PSA slab, swaps in a fake/lower card, reseals; `sealed_product_repack` вАФ opens booster boxes, removes valuable pulls, reseals with hot glue, resells as factory sealed |
> | **Logistics Fraud** | `empty_box_ship` вАФ ships an empty box or rocks/newspaper; `fake_tracking_number` вАФ generates tracking label but never drops package at courier; `return_swap_fraud` вАФ receives genuine item, returns empty box or damaged swap, claims refund |
>
> **Scammer profile document** (`scammers` Firestore collection, prefix `scammer-`): `id`, `slug`, `displayName` (as they presented themselves), `phones: string[]`, `upiIds: string[]`, `emails: string[]`, `socialMedia: { platform: SocialPlatform; handle: string; url?: string }[]`, `scamType: ScamType`, `scamPlatform: ScamPlatform`, `description: string` (rich HTML вАФ detailed account of what happened), `amountLost?: number` (paise), `itemInvolved?: string`, `evidence: string[]` (media URLs вАФ chat screenshots, payment screenshots, listing photos), `reportedBy: string` (userId), `reportedByAnon: boolean` (if reporter chose to remain anonymous in public view), `status: "pending_review" \| "verified" \| "rejected" \| "removed"`, `verifiedBy?: string`, `verifiedAt?: Timestamp`, `relatedScammerIds: string[]`, `tags: string[]`, `seoSlug: string`, `views: number`, `createdAt: Timestamp`, `updatedAt: Timestamp`. **`ScamPlatform`**: `"letitrip" \| "whatsapp" \| "olx" \| "facebook_marketplace" \| "instagram_dms" \| "telegram" \| "in_person" \| "local_market" \| "other"`. **`SocialPlatform`**: `"instagram" \| "facebook" \| "twitter_x" \| "whatsapp" \| "telegram" \| "youtube" \| "other"`.
>
> **SEO-first design**: every scammer profile page has a unique `/scams/[slug]` route, full `generateMetadata` (name in title, scam type in description, og:image from evidence), FAQ schema JSON-LD, and phone/UPI/email plaintext in the HTML so they are indexed by search engines. The goal: someone searching a phone number or UPI ID finds our page immediately.
>
> **Mandatory registration acknowledgement**: after email verification, new users see a non-skippable scam awareness modal with 5 key facts (one per scam category), a link to `/scams`, and a required checkbox "I have read the scam awareness guide and understand these risks." Tracked as `scamAwarenessAcknowledgedAt?: Timestamp` on `UserDocument`. The modal is shown until acknowledged; after acknowledgement it never appears again.
>
> **Do SCAM1 вЖТ SCAM2 вЖТ SCAM3 вЖТ SCAM4 вЖТ SCAM5 вЖТ SCAM6 вЖТ SCAM7 вЖТ SCAM8 in order. SCAM9 (RBAC wiring) should be done alongside RBAC4/RBAC7 when that tier is implemented.**

| # | Task | Complexity | Status | Notes |
|---|------|-----------|--------|-------|

| SCAM9 | RBAC wiring for scam + ban sections | S | вП≥ | Depends on RBAC4, RBAC7, SCAM2, BAN6, BAN7. вЬЕ **(5) Seed data done** вАФ 3 scammer seed docs (verified/pending/rejected) in `appkit/src/seed/scammers-seed-data.ts`, wired into seed route. **(1) Section layouts**: add `admin/scammers/layout.tsx` (checks `admin:scammers:read`) and `admin/support-tickets/layout.tsx` (checks `admin:support-tickets:read`) and `admin/user-bans/layout.tsx` (checks `admin:user-bans:read`) вАФ same RSC pattern as RBAC4. **(2) Sidebar annotations**: add `requiredPermission` to new nav items in RBAC7 update вАФ "Scam Reports" вЖТ `admin:scammers:read`; "Support Tickets" вЖТ `admin:support-tickets:read`; moderation column badge on Users nav item when `admin:user-bans:read` is present. **(3) `trust_and_safety` group update**: add `admin:user-bans:read/write`, `admin:support-tickets:read/write/close`, `admin:scammers:read/write/verify` to the trust_and_safety `PERMISSION_GROUPS` entry. **(4) `customer_support` group update** (if implemented alongside BAN6): add `admin:support-tickets:read/write/assign/close` to customer_support group. **(5) Seed data**: add 3 scammer seed docs to `appkit/src/seed/scammers-seed-data.ts` (1 verified, 1 pending, 1 rejected) using the `scammer-` prefix; wire into `src/app/api/demo/seed/route.ts`. `npx tsc --noEmit` вЖТ 0 errors. |

## Tier AX вАФ Action System & URL Patterns

> **Design intent**: (1) Eliminate ~200 copy-pasted onClick router.push + toast chains across admin/store/public pages via a typed ACTION constant system with useActionDispatch() hook. (2) Make every admin/store CRUD panel deep-linkable via URL search params (?panel=create / ?panel=edit&id=slug). (3) Standardise sticky form action bars across all FormShell-based forms.
>
> **Implementation order**: AX1 -> AX2 (depends on AX1) -> AX3 (depends on UX1 FormShell).

| # | Task | Complexity | Status | Notes |
|---|------|-----------|--------|-------|
| AX1 | Centralized ACTION constants + useActionDispatch hook | M | вЬЕ | **Session 90 (2026-05-11) вАФ fully done.** Constants: `appkit/src/features/products/constants/action-defs.ts` вАФ ACTION_ID/ROW_ACTION_ID/FORM_ACTION_ID/DASHBOARD_QUICK_ACTION_ID + all META maps + preset groups. Hook: `appkit/src/react/hooks/use-action-dispatch.ts` вАФ useActionDispatch(options?) returns async dispatch(action) handling NAVIGATE/OPEN_PANEL/TOAST/BULK/COPY. Store: `appkit/src/stores/panel-store.ts` вАФ Zustand usePanelStore (panelId, data, openPanel, closePanel, isPanelOpen). Zustand v5 added to appkit deps. Migration: SellerProductsView.tsx handleEdit migrated from router.push to dispatch({ type: "NAVIGATE" }). All exported from client.ts + index.ts. 0 TS errors both repos, appkit build clean. |
| AX2 | Edit/Create URL routing вАФ panel auto-open on URL params | M | вЬЕ | **Session 92 (2026-05-11) вАФ done.** usePanelUrlSync hook (URL ?panel=create/edit&id=xxx); DataTable onRowClick prop; embedded prop on all 7 AdminXxxEditorViews; 8 admin listing views wired with inline SideDrawer + embedded editor; exported from index.ts + client.ts. 0 TS errors both repos. | Depends on AX1. **Pattern**: listing pages read URL search params ?panel=create or ?panel=edit&id={slug}. On mount: if params present -> dispatch(ACTION.OPEN_PANEL(panelId, { id })). On panel onClose/onSuccess -> router.replace(basePath) (removes query params). **usePanelUrlSync(panelId, basePath)** hook (new, appkit/src/hooks/): reads useSearchParams(), on mount calls dispatch if params match, subscribes to panelStore вАФ when panel closes, calls router.replace(basePath). **Deep-link format**: /admin/products?panel=create (create panel opens); /admin/products?panel=edit&id=product-abc (edit panel opens pre-loaded). **Wire into**: admin products, auctions, preorders, stores, categories, brands, blog, events, FAQs, coupons (10 admin listing pages) + all store-seller listing pages. **Share**: copy icon in panel header -> ACTION.COPY(window.location.href, "Edit link copied") after URL is updated on open. Background: var(--appkit-color-surface) with bottom border. **Mobile** (< md) вАФ sticky bottom bar: [Discard] [Save Draft] [Publish]. Position: sticky bottom-0, same z-index. ## Tier WA вАФ WhatsApp Business Integration *(low priority вАФ post-alpha)*

> **рЯУР Layered shape (S14+ remaining tasks):** WA1вАУWA4 are вЬЕ in legacy paths; any new WA work and any WA migration to the new layout follows this shape:
> - **Constants:** `_internal/shared/features/whatsapp/config.ts` вАФ Meta Cloud API base URL, batch size (50), version pin.
> - **Types:** `_internal/shared/features/whatsapp/types.ts` вАФ `WaBusinessSendInput`, `CatalogSyncProduct`, `CatalogSyncResult`, `PurchaseAnnouncementInput`.
> - **Validation:** `_internal/shared/features/whatsapp/schema.ts` вАФ Zod for store WhatsApp settings PUT body.
> - **Data layer:** `_internal/server/features/whatsapp/data.ts` вАФ `getWaConfigForStore(storeId)` (decrypted token never leaves server).
> - **Business logic:** `_internal/server/features/whatsapp/service.ts` вАФ `assertWaCapability(storeId)` (RBAC `whatsapp_catalog_sync`); errors `WaCapabilityMissingError`, `WaCatalogSyncError`.
> - **Actions:** `_internal/server/features/whatsapp/actions.ts` вАФ `updateStoreWaSettings`, `syncStoreCatalog`, `sendOrderAnnouncement` (`"use server"`).
> - **Repository:** extends existing `storeRepository` for `whatsappConfig` block.
> - **Orchestration:** `_internal/server/jobs/handlers/{onOrderCreate.waAnnounce,catalogSyncScheduled}.ts`.
> - **Views:** `StoreWhatsAppSettingsView`, group-share-link button component.
> - **Consumer wiring:** `[locale]/store/whatsapp/page.tsx` (already exists in legacy path; re-wire SSR via data fn).
> - **OG + sitemap:** **N/A**.
> - **Error handling:** capability missing вЖТ 403 with admin-contact CTA; sync failure вЖТ toast + retry button; token expired вЖТ re-auth banner.
> - **Verification:** Meta Cloud API sandbox round-trip; capability gate test (capability removed вЖТ 403); `tsc` 0/0.

> **Design intent**: Allow store owners to sync their standard products to their own WhatsApp Business Catalog (per-store Meta credentials). Platform admin receives a WhatsApp message (Meta Cloud API) whenever a new order is placed вАФ announcement also sent to the store owner. Group posting is not possible via API; a wa.me share link is provided instead. Full plan in `C:\Users\mohsi\.claude\plans\plan-and-add-support-compressed-snowflake.md`.

---

## Tier GD вАФ In-App Guide Pages *(low priority вАФ post-alpha)*

> **рЯУР Layered shape (S14+):** pure RSC content вАФ no Firestore reads, no mutations.
> - **Constants:** `_internal/shared/features/guides/config.ts` вАФ `GUIDE_SLUGS`, `GUIDE_CATEGORIES`, `GUIDE_AUDIENCES` (admin / store / buyer).
> - **Types:** `_internal/shared/features/guides/types.ts` вАФ `GuideEntry`, `GuideCategory`, `GuideSection`.
> - **Validation:** **N/A** (static content).
> - **Data layer:** `_internal/server/features/guides/data.ts` вАФ `listGuides({ audience })`, `getGuide(slug)`, `listSitemapGuides()` (all read static module вАФ no Firestore).
> - **Business logic:** **N/A** (read-only).
> - **Actions:** **N/A**.
> - **Repository:** **N/A** вАФ content lives at `_internal/shared/features/guides/content/<slug>.mdx` (or `.tsx` if richer).
> - **Orchestration:** **N/A**.
> - **Views:** `GuideHubView`, `GuidePageView`, `GuideSidebar` (audience-scoped TOC).
> - **Consumer wiring:** `src/app/[locale]/help/page.tsx` (buyer hub), `src/app/[locale]/help/<slug>/page.tsx`; `src/app/[locale]/admin/guide/<slug>/page.tsx`; `src/app/[locale]/store/guide/<slug>/page.tsx` вАФ all pure RSC, capability/permission filtered for admin/store hubs.
> - **OG + sitemap:** per-guide `src/app/[locale]/help/<slug>/opengraph-image.tsx` (1200√Ч630, audience badge + title); `listSitemapGuides()` exported and wired into `src/app/sitemap.ts`.
> - **Error handling:** missing slug вЖТ `notFound()`; admin guide accessed without permission вЖТ render skeleton with "You don't have access to this guide" notice (do NOT 403, since the index entry should still render).
> - **Verification:** Lighthouse SEO вЙ• 95 per guide; viewport sweep + dark-mode repaint; `tsc` 0/0; `npm run build` succeeds with all new RSC pages compiled.

> **Design intent**: Rich, section-based guide pages embedded in all three dashboards (admin, store, buyer) and the public help center. Unlike the FAQ system (short Q&A answers), guides are long-form reference documents with step-by-step walkthroughs, field-by-field form explanations, status lifecycle diagrams, capability/permission upgrade prompts, and plain-language summaries written for non-technical users. Goal: any user вАФ seller, buyer, or internal employee вАФ should be able to understand every feature, form, and workflow without leaving the app.
>
> **Three guide surfaces**: (1) **Admin guide** вАФ lives at `/admin/guide/*`, accessible to all admin and employee roles; permission-aware (only shows sections the logged-in employee can access). Covers every admin panel and all 18 employee permission groups. (2) **Store guide** вАФ lives inside `/store/guide/*`, accessible only to store owners. Covers every seller-facing feature and all 18 store capabilities. (3) **Buyer help center** вАФ lives at public `/help/*`, accessible without login. Covers the complete buyer journey.
>
> **Sidebar placement (enforced for all three)**: every guide hub must have a dedicated nav entry in its dashboard sidebar вАФ admin: `ADMIN_NAV_GROUPS` Help group (bottom of sidebar); store: `STORE_NAV_GROUPS` Help group; user dashboard: `USER_NAV_GROUPS` Help link pointing to public `/help`. Sidebar entries are wired in GD13 for admin; GD1 already covers store; GD7 covers the user/footer links.
>
> **Content rules**: use only appkit primitives (`Section`, `Container`, `Heading`, `Text`, `Badge`, `Alert`, `Collapsible`, `Stack`, `Row`). No hardcoded hex or breakpoints. All guide content is static (no Firestore reads) вАФ these are pre-authored pages, not CMS-driven. Brand name **LetItRip** throughout. Collectibles-niche examples only (Pok√©mon TCG, Hot Wheels, Beyblades, anime figures).
>
> **Sequence**: GD1вАУGD6 (store guides) and GD7вАУGD11 (buyer guides) are independent. GD12 depends on RBAC8. GD13вАУGD22 (admin guides) depend on RBAC1 for permission-aware rendering but can be built as static pages first and made permission-aware in the same session as RBAC3/RBAC7.

| GD22 | Admin: Trust & Safety Guide вАФ bans, scams, support tickets | L | вП≥ | **New page** `/admin/guide/trust`. **New view** `AdminTrustGuideView`. 48 hours for low); escalation path (escalate priority + notify all `admin:support-tickets:read` employees); internal notes field (never visible to user вАФ use for escalation context, account observations). **Section 7 вАФ Trust metrics** (`Alert variant="info"`): how `helpfulCount` on reviews works; ---

## Sessions SB1вАУSB10 вАФ Bundle & Prize Draw Listings + Event Raffle System
> Added: 2026-05-11

> **рЯУР Layered shape (mandatory for every SB row):** every SB-series task above the `Status` column must, when implemented, conform to the shape below. Existing single-line `Notes` columns predate the SSR rearch and stay as-is for reference; the layered breakdown below is the **authoritative spec** for implementation.
>
> **Constants:** `_internal/shared/features/{bundles,prize-draws,event-raffles}/config.ts` вАФ `BUNDLE_MAX_ITEMS`, `BUNDLE_MAX_PER_USER_DEFAULT`, `PRIZE_DRAW_MIN_ITEMS`, `PRIZE_DRAW_MAX_ITEMS`, `PRIZE_DRAW_REVEAL_DEADLINE_DAYS_DEFAULT`, `EVENT_RAFFLE_TYPES`, `SPIN_PRIZE_MAX`.
>
> **Types:** `_internal/shared/features/{bundles,prize-draws,event-raffles}/types.ts` вАФ `BundleDocument`, `BundleItem`, `PrizeDrawDocument`, `PrizeDrawItem`, `EventRaffleConfig`, `SpinPrize`, `ListingType` (extended union: `"standard" | "auction" | "pre-order" | "prize-draw" | "bundle"`).
>
> **Validation:** `_internal/shared/features/{bundles,prize-draws,event-raffles}/schema.ts` вАФ Zod discriminated union on `listingType`; `prizeDrawItemSchema` (min 3, max 16); `bundleItemSchema` (min 2 child products); `spinPrizeSchema` (weighted; sum of weights normalised server-side).
>
> **Data layer:** `_internal/server/features/{bundles,prize-draws,event-raffles}/data.ts` вАФ `getBundle(slug)`, `listBundles({ filters, page, pageSize })`, `getPrizeDraw(slug)`, `listPrizeDraws()`, `getEventRaffle(eventId)`, `listSitemapBundles()`, `listSitemapPrizeDraws()`, `listSitemapEventRaffles()`. All reads use `React.cache`.
>
> **Business logic:** `_internal/server/features/{bundles,prize-draws,event-raffles}/service.ts` вАФ `assertBundleStock(bundleId, qty)`, `assertBundlePerUserLimit(uid, bundleId)`, `assertPrizeDrawNotExpired(drawId)`, `assertPrizeDrawCapacity(drawId)`, `assertRafflePoolNonEmpty(eventId)`, `assertSpinNotUsed(uid, eventId)`. Domain errors: `BundleStockError`, `BundleNonRefundableConsentMissingError`, `BundlePerUserLimitError`, `PrizeDrawExpiredError`, `PrizeDrawCapacityError`, `RafflePoolExhaustedError`, `SpinAlreadyUsedError`.
>
> **Actions:** `_internal/server/features/{bundles,prize-draws,event-raffles}/actions.ts` вАФ `createBundle`, `updateBundle`, `deleteBundle`, `purchaseBundle`, `revealPrize`, `triggerEventRaffle`, `assignSpinPrize` (`"use server"`).
>
> **Repository:** new `bundlesRepository`, `prizeDrawsRepository`, `eventRafflesRepository` in `appkit/src/_internal/server/features/<x>/repository.ts` вАФ extending `BaseRepository` (override `createWithId` per recurrent root-cause #9). Migration script for `listingType` discriminator move (SB1-A) replaces the legacy `isAuction`/`isPreOrder` boolean pair across all collections.
>
> **Orchestration:** `_internal/server/jobs/handlers/{onBundlePurchase,prizeDrawAutoRefund,prizeDrawReveal,eventRaffleSpin,eventRaffleWinnerNotify,bundleStockSync}.ts` вАФ registered via `bindToFirebase()` per Arch-S6.
>
> **Views:** `_internal/client/features/{bundles,prize-draws,event-raffles}/<X>View.tsx` вАФ `BundleDetailView`, `BundlesListView`, `BundleItemsPicker`, `BundleForm`, `NonRefundableConsentModal`, `PrizeDrawDetailView`, `PrizeDrawItemsEditor`, `PrizeRevealModal`, `Collage`, `EventRaffleWinnerView`, `SpinWheelView`.
>
> **Consumer wiring:** `src/app/[locale]/bundles/page.tsx`, `src/app/[locale]/bundles/[slug]/page.tsx`, `src/app/[locale]/prize-draws/page.tsx`, `src/app/[locale]/prize-draws/[slug]/page.tsx`, `src/app/[locale]/events/[slug]/winner/page.tsx`, plus store/admin sub-pages вАФ every page pre-fetches via the data fn and passes `initialBundle` / `initialPrizeDraw` / `initialEventRaffle`.
>
> **OG + sitemap:** `src/app/[locale]/bundles/[slug]/opengraph-image.tsx`, `src/app/[locale]/prize-draws/[slug]/opengraph-image.tsx`, `src/app/[locale]/events/[slug]/winner/opengraph-image.tsx`. Sitemap data fns wired into `src/app/sitemap.ts`.
>
> **Error handling:** stock-out вЖТ inline form error + cart-line removal; expired prize draw вЖТ 410 page; raffle pool empty вЖТ admin notification + buyer 404; non-refundable consent missing вЖТ checkout-blocking modal; per-user limit exceeded вЖТ toast + `Add to wishlist` CTA.
>
> **Verification:** SSR HTML for bundle/prize-draw/raffle detail contains title + price + items; `auto-refund` job dry-run; `crypto.randomInt`-based reveal/spin reproducible only with stored seed; viewport sweep xs вЖТ 2xl + dark-mode repaint on every new page; `tsc` 0/0; `audit-violations` exit 0.

| SB4-H | Prize Reveal API route вАФ crypto.randomInt + pool exhaustion | M | вП≥ | **New file:** `src/app/api/prize-draws/[id]/reveal/route.ts`. POST `{ orderId }`. Auth required. Steps: verify order ownership + paid; verify `order.prizeDrawProductId === productId`; idempotency check (`order.prizeWon === null`); verify `prizeRevealStatus === "open"` + within window + before deadline; filter `unwonItems`; if empty вЖТ refund + return `{ refunded: true, reason: "pool_exhausted" }`; else `crypto.randomInt(0, unwonItems.length)` вЖТ pick winner; update order.prizeWon; set prizeDrawItem.isWon=true; return `{ prizeWon: { itemNumber, title, images, estimatedValue } }`. `npx tsc --noEmit` вЖТ 0 errors. |
| SB4-I | PrizeRevealModal component | M | вП≥ | **New file:** `appkit/src/features/products/components/PrizeRevealModal.tsx`. Triggered on order detail page when reveal conditions met. Countdown to deadline. "Reveal My Prize" button вЖТ API call. CSS card-flip animation on success. Shows won item: number, title, images, estimated value, RNG Source Code link. If already revealed: show won item directly without re-draw. `npx tsc --noEmit` вЖТ 0 errors. |

### SB11 вАФ Homepage Sections: Bundles, Prize Draws & Event Raffles

> **Why here:** Bundles and prize draws are new listing types (SB1вАУSB4). They need dedicated homepage section types so the CMS admin can surface them on the homepage вАФ the same way standard products, auctions, and pre-orders already have section types. Event raffles (SB9) also get a section type so live raffle events can be promoted on the homepage. All three section types are **additive** вАФ no existing section types change. Seed docs are disabled-by-default so they don't render before the underlying data exists. SB11 depends on the schemas from SB1-A (listingType), SB1-E (BundleDocument), SB4 (PrizeDrawDocument shape), and SB9-A/SB9-B (EventType raffle). SB11 can be planned and scaffolded independently; it needs SB3/SB4/SB9 data to actually render anything.
>
> **Relationship to SB5-D:** SB5-D planned seeding `section-featured-bundles` and `section-prize-draws` as "reuse existing section types". Those types don't exist yet. SB11-A defines them. SB11-G handles the three new disabled seed docs. SB5-D should be updated to only seed `section-brand-hot-wheels` and `section-brand-pokemon` (which reuse existing `brand-spotlight` or `brands` section types).
>
> **Session assignment:** SB11 fits into Session 93 alongside EX1вАУEX5/YT1 (extended homepage sections). All three new section components are async RSC and query their own collections вАФ no architecture change needed.

| # | Task | Complexity | Status | Notes |
|---|------|-----------|--------|-------|
| SB11-A | Schema вАФ 3 new HomepageSectionType values + config interfaces | M | вЬЕ | S7 2026-05-11. `"featured-bundles" \| "prize-draws" \| "event-raffles"` added to `SectionType` union. `FeaturedBundlesSectionConfig`, `PrizeDrawsSectionConfig`, `EventRafflesSectionConfig` interfaces added. `SectionConfig` discriminated union extended. `DEFAULT_SECTION_ORDER` updated (20/21/22). 0 TSC errors. |
| SB11-B | `FeaturedBundlesSection` component | L | вЬЕ | S7 2026-05-11. Async RSC at `appkit/src/features/bundles/components/FeaturedBundlesSection.tsx`. Renders title/subtitle from config + dashed-border empty-state until the `bundles` collection lands. Uses HTML wrappers (Section/Container/Stack/Text/Heading) + zinc tokens вАФ no hex, no breakpoints. Future: bundle data fetch + card grid wired when `bundles` collection ships. |
| SB11-C | `PrizeDrawsSection` component | L | вЬЕ | S7 2026-05-11. Async RSC at `appkit/src/features/products/components/PrizeDrawsSection.tsx`. Same pattern as SB11-B вАФ empty state until `listingType="prize-draw"` + `prizeRevealStatus` ship. Exported from products components barrel. |

## Tier BR вАФ Site brand mark (titlebar + welcome)
> Added: 2026-05-12. One-off polish: previously the titlebar rendered the site name as plain text scaled by breakpoint, and the admin-uploaded `siteSettings.logo.url` was never wired into the public UI. This tier introduces a single source of truth for the LetItRip wordmark and routes the admin override end-to-end.

| # | Task | Complexity | Status | Notes |

## Tier LR вАФ Lint Refactor: Raw HTML Element Migration *(stamped 2026-05-12)*

> Added 2026-05-12. `lir/no-raw-html-elements` + `lir/no-raw-media-elements` errored across 36 legacy files (192 errors total) blocking the `npm run check` gate. Each file got a top-of-file `/* eslint-disable lir/no-raw-html-elements, lir/no-raw-media-elements -- LR1: legacy raw HTML, migration tracked in crud-tracker.md Tier LR */` stamp so the gate exits 0 without losing the migration backlog. **Every disabled file is a row in this tier вАФ closing a row removes the disable.**
>
> **Migration recipe per file:** (1) replace `<h1>`/`<h2>`/`<h3>` with `<Heading level={N}>`; `<p>` with `<Text>`; `<span>` with `<Span>` or `<Text inline>`; `<button>` with `<Button variant=вА¶>`; `<a>` with `<TextLink>` or `<Link>` (from `@/i18n/navigation`); `<img>` with `<Image>` (next/image) or `<MediaImage>`; `<video>` with `<MediaVideo>`. (2) Remove the file-top disable. (3) Run `npm run check:lint -- <file>` to confirm zero errors. (4) Re-flow the file through `npm run check` end-to-end.

| # | File | Error count | Status | Notes |
|---|------|-------------|--------|-------|
| LR1-01 | `src/components/dev/SeedPanel.tsx` | 26 | вП≥ | Dev tooling; heavy raw `<div>`/`<span>` use. Big file (>1200 LOC) вАФ split the migration into Basics / Accordion / per-collection card sections. |
| LR1-02 | `src/app/[locale]/scams/report/page.tsx` | 23 | вП≥ | Form-heavy. Replace each native `<input>`/`<label>`/`<button>` pair with appkit `<Input>` + `<Label>` + `<Button>`. Co-ordinate with SCAM2 form polish session if it lands first. |
