### LR2 вАФ Appkit lint backlog *(separate from letitrip src)*

> Discovered 2026-05-12. `npm run check`'s `check:lint` step only lints `src/**` (letitrip). Running `npx eslint src/**/*.{ts,tsx}` inside `appkit/` surfaces **404 errors** that the gate doesn't see today. Adding appkit lint to the gate now would block all forward work; this row tracks the cleanup so it gets done.

| # | Rule | Count | Status | Migration approach |
|---|------|-------|--------|--------------------|
| LR2-A | `@typescript-eslint/no-explicit-any` | 228 | вП≥ | Each `any` is a type-debt entry. Sweep by feature (e.g. `appkit/src/features/products/**`, then `auctions/**`). Per file: replace with concrete type, `unknown`, or generic. Some inevitable in adapter layers вАФ leave `// eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-explicit-any` with a `LR2-A: <reason>` comment. |
| LR2-B | `@typescript-eslint/no-unused-vars` | 150 | вП≥ | Mostly unused params + leftover imports from refactors. `--fix` handles many; the rest are intentional (destructured `_ignored`) and need `_` prefix. |
| LR2-C | `@typescript-eslint/no-empty-object-type` | 21 | вП≥ | `interface Foo {}` placeholders left over from incremental design. Either give them a body or replace with `type Foo = Record<string, never>`. |
| LR2-D | Other (`prefer-const`, malformed JSDoc) | 5 | вП≥ | One-off cleanups. |

**Activation plan**: once LR2-A/B/C land, wire appkit eslint into the root `npm run check:lint` so future regressions block the gate.

## Tier OG вАФ OpenGraph Image Coverage *(post-alpha; backlog audit)*

> **Design intent:** every public detail page (one resource at one URL) ships an `opengraph-image.tsx` so social shares render rich previews. As of 2026-05-12, 7 detail families have OG images (products, auctions, pre-orders, stores, brands, blog, events). This tier closes the gap on existing routes; OG tasks for **new** resources (bundles, prize-draws, scams, guides, etc.) live with their own tier and are not duplicated here.
>
> **рЯУР Layered shape (S14+):** OG tasks are pure consumer-wiring + verification вАФ most layers **N/A**. *Data layer*: reuse the existing per-feature `data.ts` getter (`getCategoryBySlug`, `faqRepository.getBySlug`, etc.). *Consumer wiring*: the new `opengraph-image.tsx` file itself, edge runtime, `ImageResponse` 1200√Ч630. *OG + sitemap*: this row IS the OG task; sitemap entries already exist on the listing data fns. *Error handling*: missing resource вЖТ fall back to default OG image at `src/app/opengraph-image.tsx`. *Verification*: `curl -sI http://localhost:3000/<route>/opengraph-image` вЖТ `200 image/png` + visual check in Twitter/Facebook debugger; `npm run build` includes the new edge route.

| # | Task | Complexity | Status | Notes |
|---|------|-----------|--------|-------|
| OG1 | `categories/[slug]/[tab]/sort/[sortKey]/page/[page]/opengraph-image.tsx` | S | вП≥ | Cover image background + category name + product count badge. Data: existing `getCategoryBySlug` from `_internal/server/features/categories/data.ts`. Edge runtime. Verification: `curl -sI .../opengraph-image` вЖТ 200 image/png. |
| OG2 | `faq/[slug]/opengraph-image.tsx` | S | вП≥ | Q&A snippet card вАФ question as title, first 240 chars of answer as body. Data: existing `faqRepository.getBySlug`. Verify the route file path matches actual implementation (FAQ slug route may live elsewhere вАФ confirm before scaffolding). |
| OG3 | `user/[slug]/opengraph-image.tsx` | S | вП≥ | Public user profile card вАФ display name + avatar + role badge (verified seller / buyer). **Verify with author whether `/user/[slug]` is a public route before implementing** вАФ store profiles already covered by stores OG. |
| OG4 | Sub-listing detail OG | S | вП≥ | Verify route exists first (`sub-listings/[slug]/page.tsx` or similar). If yes: scaffold OG with parent listing context + sublisting title. If no: close as N/A with one-line note. |
| OG5 | Audit script: `appkit/scripts/verify-og-coverage.mjs` | M | вП≥ | Walks `src/app/[locale]/**/page.tsx`, lists every `[slug]`/`[id]` dynamic detail route, checks for sibling `opengraph-image.tsx`, exits non-zero on missing. Wire into CI gate alongside `verify-entries.mjs`. Output format: one line per missing OG. Verification: run on current tree вЖТ must report only the OG1вАУOG4 known gaps + every new resource not yet shipped. |

## Tier EMG вАФ Emerging Patterns *(holding bay for code/copy mentions without tasks)*

> **Process note:** whenever a session notices a feature, payment method, integration, or content type that is referenced in code or copy but has no implementation task, **append a row here in the same session вАФ do not wait for triage**. EMG is the holding bay until a feature graduates into its own tier or scheduled session. Re-scan triggers: any new mention surfaced by `grep` for keywords (`EMI`, `installment`, `gift card`, `loyalty`, `live chat`, `affiliate`, `referral`, `crypto`, `subscription`, `B2B`, `wholesale`); any FAQ or seed-copy mention of a flow with no code path; any partial implementation in `letitrip.in/functions/src/` not surfaced in the public app. Each row carries the full layered shape (or explicit **N/A**) so it is implementation-ready when scheduled.

| # | Task | Complexity | Status | Notes |
|---|------|-----------|--------|-------|
| EMG1 | EMI / installment payment at checkout | L | рЯОѓ | **Triage 2026-05-12 (S45):** **ready-to-graduate.** Full layered shape exists in this row + Razorpay supports it via existing webhook + `_internal/shared/features/payments/` would be a new sub-tree (no conflicts). When scheduled, lift this row out of EMG into a new **Tier PAY** (Payments Extensions) or extend **Tier V** at the Versatility level. Recommend pairing with EMG3 (gift cards) so payments work is a single multi-session arc instead of two staggered ones. **Discovery:** `appkit/src/seed/faq-seed-data.ts` line 571 ("UPI, COD, EMI"); `src/components/dev/SeedPanel.tsx:874` ("Payment Methods FAQs (UPI, COD, EMI)"). **Verified 2026-05-12:** zero implementation across `appkit/src/` and `src/` (grep `EMI\|installment` вЖТ only seed copy). Razorpay supports EMI via `payment_capture` config + EMI plans; Bajaj Finserv is a viable alt provider. **рЯУР Layered shape:** *Constants:* `_internal/shared/features/payments/config.ts` вАФ `EMI_MIN_CART_VALUE_PAISE`, `EMI_PROVIDERS`, `EMI_TENURES_MONTHS`. *Types:* `_internal/shared/features/payments/types.ts` вАФ `EmiPlan`, `EmiOption`, `PaymentMethodWithEmi`. *Validation:* `_internal/shared/features/payments/schema.ts` вАФ Zod for EMI selection at checkout. *Data layer:* `_internal/server/features/payments/data.ts` вАФ `getEmiPlansForAmount(amountPaise)`. *Business logic:* `_internal/server/features/payments/service.ts` вАФ `assertEmiEligible(cartTotal)`; error `EmiNotEligibleError`. *Actions:* extend `createOrder` to accept EMI plan; new `recordEmiSelection`. *Repository:* extend `ordersRepository` `paymentMethod` enum to include `EMI_*`. *Orchestration:* `_internal/server/jobs/handlers/onEmiOrderCreate.ts` (server-side polling for EMI capture confirmation); reuse Razorpay webhook for capture event. *Views:* `EmiOptionsList` (checkout panel), `EmiBadge` on product card ("EMI from вВєX/mo"). *Consumer wiring:* `CheckoutRouteClient.tsx` payment-method picker; `ProductDetailPageView` EMI badge. *OG + sitemap:* **N/A**. *Error handling:* ineligible cart вЖТ option hidden + tooltip; provider failure вЖТ fallback to standard payment + toast. *Verification:* Razorpay test EMI flow end-to-end (test card); product card badge renders only when `price вЙ• EMI_MIN_CART_VALUE_PAISE`; `tsc` 0/0. |
